# ezEdits Docs | ezEdits Wiki

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-537c6419c189007102c716ce43fd9ac9f3fb6f2c%252Flogofinal5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d19a429c&sv=2)

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits#what-is-ezedits)

What is ezEdits?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------

ezEdits is a WorldEdit/FastAsyncWorldEdit (WE/FAWE) extension plugin which adds numerous new commands, patterns, masks, and tools to help you make amazing creations!

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits#links)

Links


-------------------------------------------------------

*   Get ezEdits (**Available Now**): [Ko-Fi](https://ko-fi.com/ezedits)
     or [Patreon](https://www.patreon.com/ezedits)
    
*   Discord: [https://discord.gg/NfT3vyeKu5](https://discord.gg/NfT3vyeKu5)
    
*   Twitter: [https://twitter.com/ezEditsMC](https://twitter.com/ezEditsMC)
    
*   Instagram: [https://www.instagram.com/ezeditsmc/](https://www.instagram.com/ezeditsmc/)
    
*   Help us improve the docs here: [https://github.com/Zeranny/ezedits-wiki](https://github.com/Zeranny/ezedits-wiki)
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits#authors)

Authors

The plugin is written by [@eztaK\_red](https://linktr.ee/eztak)
 and [@Zeranny](https://x.com/zeranny)
.

# Installing | ezEdits Wiki

ezEdits is installed like any other plugin, but requires either WorldEdit or FastAsyncWorldEdit to already be installed (only one, not both).

*   [WorldEdit](https://modrinth.com/plugin/worldedit)
    
*   [FastAsyncWorldEdit](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/fastasyncworldedit.13932/)
    

Currently we support Minecraft 1.20+ but it may work on older versions. If you use 1.20.5+ make sure to update your Java to at least 21.

Do note that Paper is the targetted server software for our support and you may have compatibility issues when using a non-Paper fork.

**You can obtain the .jar file from Discord by supporting us on Patreon/Ko-Fi.**

*   Once you have the Silver/Gold rank in Discord, run `/download` in a Supporter channel to receive the .jar file
    

Simply drop the .jar file into your plugins folder and run your server as normal. An "ezEdits" folder containing a config.yml file will be created which you can edit.

[PreviousezEdits Docs](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits)
[NextPermissions](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/getting-started/permissions)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Permissions | ezEdits Wiki

Permissions are grouped into permpacks which can be granted with `ezedits.permpack.***`

Permission

Description

Permpack

ezedits.general.wiki

**/ezedits wiki** Prints the link for this wiki in chat

Basic

ezedits.general.info

**/ezedits info** Prints basic plugin info in chat

Basic

ezedits.general.quiet

**/ezedits quiet** Toggles on/off some of the chat messages from ezEdits

Basic

ezedits.admin.reload

**/ezedits reload** Reloads the config

Admin

ezedits.array

**//ezarray** Places multiple structures sequentially along a path

Advanced

ezedits.brush.array

**//ezbr array** Allows placing multiple shapes or 3d structures along a drawn path

Advanced

ezedits.brush.gradient

**//ezbr gradient** Binds the gradient brush to an item

Intermediate

ezedits.brush.gradientstroke

**//ezbr gradientstroke** Binds the gradient stroke brush to an item

Intermediate

ezedits.brush.paletteshift

**//ezbr paletteshift** Binds the palette shift brush to an item

Intermediate

ezedits.brush.scatter

**//ezbr scatter** Allows placing multiple shapes or 3d structures in an area

Advanced

ezedits.debug

**//ezdebug ...** Various debug commands. Not required for normal use

Admin

ezedits.debug.loadingbar

**//ezdebug clearLoadingBars** Clears any active progress bar on screen.

Basic

ezedits.deform.hexagonalize

**//ezdeform hexagonalize** Deforms the blocks in selection into hexagonal pillars

Intermediate

ezedits.deform.noise

**//ezdeform noise** Deforms the blocks in selection based on a given noise

Intermediate

ezedits.deform.rotate

**//ezdeform rotate** Rotates the blocks in selection

Basic

ezedits.deform.voronoialize

**//ezdeform voronoialize** Deforms the blocks in a selection into voronoi cells

Intermediate

ezedits.deform.voronoialize2

**//ezdeform voronoialize2** Deforms the blocks in a selection into voronoi cells approximating the input shapes

Intermediate

ezedits.deform.voxelize

**//ezdeform voxelize** Deforms the blocks in a selection into voxels

Intermediate

ezedits.flow.flowfield

**//ezflowfield** Generates a flowfield within a selection

Intermediate

ezedits.flow.flowline

**//ezflowline** Creates a single flow line from the player position

Intermediate

ezedits.gen.cone

**//ezshapes cone** Generates a Cone at the player's position

Basic

ezedits.gen.polydome

**//ezshapes polydome** Generates a Polydome at the player's position

Basic

ezedits.gen.polygon

**//ezshapes polygon** Generates a Polygon at the player's position

Basic

ezedits.gen.square

**//ezshapes square** Generates a Square at the player's position

Basic

ezedits.gen.tetrahedron

**//ezshapes tetrahedron** Generates a Tetrahedron at the player's position

Basic

ezedits.gen.torus

**//ezshapes Torus** Generates a Torus at the player's position

Basic

ezedits.mask.aim

**#aim** Masks to blocks matching the target block

Basic

ezedits.mask.attached

**#attached** Masks to blocks touching adjacent blocks

Basic

ezedits.mask.current

**#current** Represents your current global mask

Basic

ezedits.mask.fullblock

**#fullblock** Masks to blocks which occupy a full block of space

Basic

ezedits.mask.infested

**#infested** Masks to blocks which contain a silverfish

Basic

ezedits.mask.light

**#truelight | #blocklight** Masks to block matching a light level range. Truelight includes skylight Blocklight only considers light from blocks

Basic

ezedits.mask.near

**#near** Masks to blocks withing a given 3D range of the inner mask

Intermediate

ezedits.mask.noise

**#eznoisemask** Masks to blocks at positions where the given noise is above the given threshold

Intermediate

ezedits.mask.palette

**#palette | #fuzzypalette** Masks to blocks within the given palette. Fuzzypalette ignores block states

Intermediate

ezedits.mask.selection

**#savedselection** Masks to blocks within the region of a saved selection

Intermediate

ezedits.mask.vectorgradient

**#vectorgradientmask** Masks to blocks at positions along a given vector which are above the gradient threshold

Intermediate

ezedits.noise.delete

**//eznoise delete** Deletes a saved noise preset

Intermediate

ezedits.noise.list

**//eznoise list** Lists all saved noise presets

Intermediate

ezedits.noise.print

**//eznoise print** Prints the parameters of a saved noise preset

Intermediate

ezedits.noise.save

**//eznoise save** Saves a noise preset

Intermediate

ezedits.palettes.decode

**//ezpalette decode** Prints the blocks of a given encoded palette string.

Intermediate

ezedits.palettes.delete

**//ezpalette delete** Deletes a saved palette

Intermediate

ezedits.palettes.encode

**//ezpalette encode** Encodes a palette into a shorter text string

Intermediate

ezedits.palettes.fetch

**//ezpalette fetch** Fetches blocks from the world or player's hotbar and saves as a palette

Intermediate

ezedits.palettes.list

**//ezpalette list** Lists all saved palettes

Intermediate

ezedits.palettes.place

**//ezpalette place** Places a saved palette into the world

Intermediate

ezedits.palettes.print

**//ezpalette print** Prints the blocks of a saved palette

Intermediate

ezedits.palettes.save

**//ezpalette save** Saves a palette

Intermediate

ezedits.palettes.swap

**//ezpalette swap** Swaps all the blocks matching with the corresponding block in another palette

Intermediate

ezedits.pattern.aim

**#aim** Uses the target block as the pattern

Basic

ezedits.pattern.noise

**#eznoisepattern** Uses a noise preset to place palette blocks

Intermediate

ezedits.pattern.palette

**#palette** Treats the blocks in a palette as if they were simply listed out

Intermediate

ezedits.pattern.selection

**#selection** Sets blocks based on what is currently in the world at the location of the saved selection. As if that area were tiled/stacked

Intermediate

ezedits.pattern.vectorgradient

**#vectorgradientpattern** Sets palette blocks along a vector with a given length

Intermediate

ezedits.region.moss

**//ezmoss** Places a layer of blocks on flat surfaces

Intermediate

ezedits.region.noisegen

**//eznoisegen ...** Uses noise to place blocks within a region

Intermediate

ezedits.region.solidslab

**//ezslabmerge** Converts double slabs into full blocks

Basic

ezedits.region.statecycle

**//ezstatecycle** Cycles a given block state for all blocks with that state

Intermediate

ezedits.region.vines

**//ezvines** Hangs blocks like vines from the given mask

Intermediate

ezedits.scatter

**//ezscatter** Scatters a shape or 3d structure across the surface of blocks within your selection

Advanced

ezedits.selection.delete

**//ezselection delete** Deletes a saved selection

Intermediate

ezedits.selection.delpos

**//-2** Removes the last point in your selection

Basic

ezedits.selection.encapsulate

**//encapsulate** Resizes an existing selection to the smallest cuboid containing matching blocks

Basic

ezedits.selection.encapsulatenear

**//encapsulatenear** Creates a cuboid selection of the smallest size to contain nearby matching blocks

Basic

ezedits.selection.here

**//selhere** Moves selection to the player

Basic

ezedits.selection.invert

**//selinvert** Reverses the order of points in a selection

Basic

ezedits.selection.list

**//ezselection list** Lists all saved selections

Intermediate

ezedits.selection.load

**//selload** Loads a saved selection

Intermediate

ezedits.selection.next

**//next** Moves a selection by its own size in a given direction

Basic

ezedits.selection.save

**//ezselection save** Saves the current selection

Intermediate

ezedits.smooth.deflate

**//ezdeflate** Contracts the blocks in a selection

Basic

ezedits.smooth.ezsmooth

**//ezsmooth** Smooths a selection in 3D

Intermediate

ezedits.smooth.inflate

**//ezinflate** Expands the blocks in a selection

Basic

ezedits.smooth.smoothblocks

**//ezsmoothblocks** Smooths a region using stairs, slabs, and walls

Advanced

ezedits.spline.basic

**//ezspline basic** Generates a simple cylindrical spline

Intermediate

Intermediate

# Palette Commands | ezEdits Wiki

All sub-commands are under `//ezpalette` (`//ezp`) e.g `//ezpalette list`

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/palettes/palette-commands#ezpalette)

`//ezpalette ...`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/palettes/palette-commands#fetch-less-than-fetchmode-greater-than-less-than-palettename-greater-than-length-d-less-than-directi)

`fetch <fetchMode> <paletteName> [length] [-d <direction>] [-f]`

Fetch Palette[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/palettes/palette-commands#fetch-palette)

Saves a user-defined palette with a given name.

*   **Fetch Mode**: From where to fetch the palette blocks:
    
    *   `**WORLD**`
        
        *   Takes the blocks from the player's position
            
        
    *   `**SELECTION**`
        
        *   Takes the blocks from the player's selection
            
        *   Selection must be 1x1xN in size, where N is the desired palette length
            
        
    *   `**HOTBAR**`
        
        *   Takes blocks from the player's hotbar
            
        *   Ignores items and uses default block properties
            
        
    
*   **Length** (Default: 0): How many block to fecth. A length of 0 (default) will fetch blocks until air is reached.
    
*   **\-d** (Default: me): The direction to fetch in. Defaults to the direction the user is facing.
    
*   **\-f**: When activated, overwrites the existing palette with the same name.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252FSvT88repFEVTDXGpBaft%252Fezp_fetch.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D54d28d19-1105-443d-b0b9-5360d4fbb5a2&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fe9ed85c&sv=2)

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/palettes/palette-commands#save-less-than-palettename-greater-than-less-than-palette-greater-than-f)

`save <paletteName> <palette> [-f]`

Saves a user-defined palette with a given name.

*   **\-f**: When activated, overwrites the existing palette with the same name.
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/palettes/palette-commands#delete-less-than-palettename-greater-than)

`delete <paletteName>`

Deletes a user-defined palette matching the given name.

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/palettes/palette-commands#list-set)

`list [SET]`

*   `ALL` Lists all available palettes
    
*   `DEFAULT` Lists all default plugin palettes
    
*   `MINE` Lists all user-defined palettes
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/palettes/palette-commands#place-less-than-palette-greater-than-direction)

`place <palette> [direction]`

Places a palette in the world as a row of blocks in the given direction. Direction defaults to the direction the user is facing.

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/palettes/palette-commands#swap-less-than-sourcepalette-greater-than-less-than-targetpalette-greater-than-a-f)

`swap <sourcePalette> <targetPalette> [-a] [-f]`

Region operation which swaps the blocks of the source palette with those of the target palette.

*   **\-a**: Activate to ignore air blocks in source palette.
    
*   **\-s**: Activate to stretch the target palette to match the size of the source palette.
    
*   **\-f**: Enables fuzzy matching mode. Ignoring the block states of the source palette.
    
*   **\-b**: Copies the block states from the source palette blocks onto the target palette.
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/palettes/palette-commands#print-less-than-palette-greater-than-v)

`print <palette> [-v]`

Prints the blocks of a given palette in chat. Block list can be clicked to copy.

**\-v**: Verbose mode. Will print full block name and block states.

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/palettes/palette-commands#encode-less-than-palette-greater-than)

`encode <palette>`

Prints an encoded string representing a given palette. Click the string to copy. _Only supports vanilla Minecraft blocks._

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/palettes/palette-commands#decode-less-than-string-greater-than)

`decode <string>`

Prints the blocks of a given encoded palette string. Block list can be clicked to copy.

[PreviousDefault Palettes](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/palettes/default-palettes)
[NextNoise Explained](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/noise/noise-explained)

# Default Palettes | ezEdits Wiki

By default, palettes are saved per player. However, server admins may define a set of default palettes accessible to all players in

Copy

    plugins/ezEdits/resources/DefaultPalettes.json

We also come with a predefined set of default palettes:

* * *

# Noise Explained | ezEdits Wiki

Noise can be a complex topic for anyone who has never read into it before, but in its simplest terms, noise is a way of getting a value out of some input (usually X,Y,Z coordinates).

The place you will likely be most familiar with noise is in Minecraft's terrain generation. At every point in the world, several noise functions are combined to determine if a block should be placed, and if so, which block.

This is pretty much what we do in ezEdits, using noise to generate shapes, terrain, and textures.

Within the plugin you will find several noise types, with each having different characteristics, and Cellular specifically coming with many additional parameters you can customise.

Some of the many features that use noise include:

*   `//eznoisegen ...` - _Noisegen Commands_
    
*   `#eznoisemask` - _Masks_
    
*   `//ezbrush gradient ...` - _Brushes_
    

_Noise in ezEdits based on a modified version of FastNoiseLite, so we strongly recommend this website to experiment with noise parameters:_ [_http://auburn.github.io/FastNoiseLite/_](http://auburn.github.io/FastNoiseLite/)

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/noise/noise-explained#noise-parameters)

Noise Parameters


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each parameter and many values also has a shorthand, such as "ft" instead of "FractalType" or "Si" instead of "OpenSimplex2". Wherever this is possible, the shorthand will be shown in brackets. `Red = Parameter` `Purple = Value`

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/noise/noise-explained#noise-type)

Noise Type

Setting the Noise Type[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/noise/noise-explained#setting-the-noise-type)

Sets the type of noise to be used. This is the start of any noise and will be in the format of `Noise()`, for example `Perlin()`, where all other parameters will go between the brackets.

*   `Perlin (Pe)`
    
*   `OpenSimplex2 (Si)`
    
*   `OpenSimplex2S (Sm)`
    
*   `Value (Va)`
    
*   `ValueCubic (VC)`
    
*   `White (Wh)`
    
*   `Cellular (Ce)`
    
*   `Shard (Sh)`
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/noise/noise-explained#basic-noise-parameters)

Basic Noise Parameters

Basic Noise Parameters[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/noise/noise-explained#basic-noise-parameters-1)

*   `Seed (s)` Sets the seed value for the noise. -1 or no value will result in a random noise seed.
    
*   `Frequency (f)` Sets the frequency for the noise. A higher frequency will lead to steeper noise, a lower value will lead to smoother noise.
    
*   `Inverted (i)` Whether to invert the noise value or not. Default is false.
    
    *   `True`
        
    *   `False`
        
    
*   `ValueMapping (m)` Whether to ignore or override the value mapping. By default noise is sampled to map between 0 and 1.
    
    *   `Default (Def)`
        
    *   `None (No)`
        
    *   `Override (OR)` **If Overridden:**
        
        *   `LowerBound (l)`
            
        *   `UpperBound (u)`
            
        
    
*   `XScaling (x)` This can be used to stretch or squish the X axis.
    
*   `YScaling (y)` When using 3D noises this can be used to stretch or squish the Y axis.
    
*   `ZScaling (z)` This can be used to stretch or squish the Z axis.
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/noise/noise-explained#cellular-noise-parameters)

Cellular Noise Parameters

**Additional Cellular Noise Parameters**[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/noise/noise-explained#additional-cellular-noise-parameters)

*   `CellularJitterModifier (cJ)` Usually `0..1.0` Controls the random jitter or distribution of cellular noise nodes, with 0 being a perfect grid, and 1 being maximally "random", without overlap. Values above 1 will start to overlap their neighbours.
    
*   `CellularDistanceFunction (cD)` Controls the mathematical method used to determine the distance value for each point to its node.
    
    *   `Euclidean (e)`
        
    *   `EuclideanSq (sq)`
        
    *   `Manhattan (man)`
        
    *   `Hybrid (h)`
        
    *   `Minkovski1 (m1)`
        
    *   `Minkowvki4 (m4)`
        
    *   `Minkowski99 (m99)`
        
    *   `Rounded (r)`
        
    
*   `CellularReturnType (cR)` Controls how the distance value is modified prior to being returned. All Distance2\* values refer to the 2nd closest node instead of the closest.
    
    *   `CellValue (cell)`
        
    *   `Distance (1)`
        
    *   `DistanceSquared (sq)`
        
    *   `DistanceInverse (inv)`
        
    *   `DistanceLog (log)`
        
    *   `DistanceExp (exp)`
        
    *   `Distance2 (2)`
        
    *   `Distance2Add (2add)`
        
    *   `Distance2Add (2sub)`
        
    *   `Distance2Add (2mul)`
        
    *   `Distance2Add (2div)`
        
    *   `Distance2Sq (2sq)`
        
    *   `Distance2Inv (2inv)`
        
    *   `Distance2Log (2log)`
        
    *   `Distance2Exp (2exp)`
        
    *   `Edge (e)`
        
    *   `Rounded (r)`
        
    *   `NoiseLookup (n)` **Additional Noise Lookup Parameters:**
        
        *   `CellularNoiseLookup (cN)` When using the NoiseLookup return type, this controls the underlying noise to overlay the cellular noise upon.
            
            *   `Perlin (Pe)`
                
            *   `OpenSimplex2 (Si)`
                
            *   `OpenSimplex2S (Sm)`
                
            *   `Value (Va)`
                
            *   `ValueCubic (VC)`
                
            *   `White (Wh)`
                
            *   `Cellular (Ce)`
                
            
        *   `CellularNoiseLookupFrequency (cF)` Controls the frequency of the underlying noise.
            
        
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/noise/noise-explained#shard-noise-parameters)

Shard Noise Parameters

Additional Shard Noise Parameters[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/noise/noise-explained#additional-shard-noise-parameters)

*   `Sharpness (h)` Usually `0..1.0` Controls the pattern sharpness for Shard noise. Higher values have more defined edges within the pattern, whereas low values will appear more blurry.
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/noise/noise-explained#fractal-noise-parameters)

Fractal Noise Parameters

Fractal Noise Parameters[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/noise/noise-explained#fractal-noise-parameters-1)

*   `FractalType (fT)` Sets the type of fractal noise to be used.
    
    *   `None (N)`
        
    *   `FBm (F)`
        
    *   `Ridged (R)`
        
    *   `PingPong (P)` **Additional PingPong Fractal Parameter:**
        
        *   `PingPongStrength (fP)`
            
        
    

**If Fractal Type other than** `**None**` **selected:**

*   `Octaves (fO)` Sets the number of layers of fractal noise to be used.
    
*   `Lacunarity (fL)` Sets the scale of each fractal layer. Values >1 will effectively increase the frequency for each layer, values <1 will effectively reduce the frequency for each layer.
    
*   `Gain (fG)` Sets the relative strength of each fractal layer. Values <1 will decrease in strength for each layer, values >1 will increase.
    
*   `WeightedStrength (fW)` Sets the responsiveness of each layer's strength to the noise value.
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/noise/noise-explained#domain-warp-parameters)

Domain Warp Parameters

Domain Warp Parameters[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/noise/noise-explained#domain-warp-parameters-1)

*   `DomainWarpType (wT)` Sets the type of domain warping to be used.
    
    *   `None (N)`
        
    *   `BasicGrid (G)`
        
    *   `OpenSimplex2 (S)`
        
    *   `OpenSimplex2Reduced (R)`
        
    *   `Flow (F)`
        
    *   `Turbulence (T)`
        
    

**If Domain Warp Type other than** `**None**` **selected:**

*   `DomainWarpFreq (wF)` Sets the frequency for the domain warp.
    
*   `DomainWarpOct (wO)` Sets the number of layers for the domain warp.
    
*   `DomainWarpGain (wG)` Sets the relative strength of each domain warp layer.
    
*   `DomainWarpAmp (wA)` Sets the overall amplitude (strength) of the domain warp.
    
*   `DomainWarpFrac (wC)` Sets the domain warp specific fractal type to be used.
    
    *   `None (N)`
        
    *   `DomainWarpIndependent (I)`
        
    *   `DomainWarpProgressive (P)`
        
    
*   `DomainWarpLacunarity (wl)` Sets the scale of each domain warp layer.
    

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/noise/noise-explained#examples)

Examples


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`**Value(Seed:123,Frequency:0.04)**`

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-4e653a28c5c1cd4cab8cad82c8e9eb5937e50096%252F2024-01-10_20.38.35.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=294cec29&sv=2)

`**Cellular(cellularDistanceFunction:Euclidean,cellularReturnType:NoiseLookup,cellularNoiseLookup:Perlin,cellularNoiseLookupFrequency:0.2,Frequency:0.1)**`

_Same noise, but using all abbreviations:_ `**Ce(cD:e,cR:n,cN:Pe,cF:.2,F:.1)**`

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-ae36f180d252a466611139c3d40f0193de7b9dcb%252F2024-01-10_20.41.26.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f4b5174d&sv=2)

# Palette Shift Brush | ezEdits Wiki

* * *

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/brushes/palette-shift-brush#ezbr-paletteshift)

`//ezbr` `paletteshift`

Palette Shift Brush[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/brushes/palette-shift-brush#palette-shift-brush)

`**//ezbr paletteshift**` `**<palette>**` `**[radius]**` `**[shift]**`

Replaces blocks matching the palette with palette blocks shifted along by the given amount. For example, a shift value of 2 will replace any instances of the first palette block with the third.

*   **Palette**: Specifies the block pattern for the gradient.
    
*   **Radius** (Default: 8): Sets the radius of the brush.
    
*   **Shift** (Default: 1): The amount by which to shift blocks within palette
    

Tip: Right-clicking and left-clicking shift into opposite "directions".

* * *

[PreviousBrushes](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/brushes)
[NextPalette Gradient Brushes](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/brushes/palette-gradient-brushes)

Last updated 6 months ago

# Palettes Explained | ezEdits Wiki

Palettes in ezEdits represent a list of blocks that can be used in several commands where the order of blocks will be maintained.

Palettes can be saved and accessed using the `**#**` prefix for user-saved palettes, and `**##**` for [inbuilt preset palettes](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/palettes/default-palettes)
.

For reference, here's an example:

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-9205cfef2a7bfe1148831395905c0b9690769bbc%252Fpalette_Grayscale.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b8e52c8c&sv=2)

##Grayscale

Some of the many features that use palettes include:

*   `//eztexture ...` - [Texturing Commands](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/texturing)
    
*   `#palette` - [Palette mask](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#palette-mask)
    
*   `//ezbrush gradient ...` - [Brushes](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/brushes)
    

Palettes can be constructed as a simple list of blocks, or via several modifiers:

*   `**,**` - **Concatenate**:
    
    *   Adds one block or palette to the end of the preceding block or palette. e.g `stone,dirt` is a 2 block palette of stone and dirt. `stone,##Grayscale` is a palette made of stone and the blocks of the ##Grayscale preset palette.
        
    
*   `**-**` - **Invert**:
    
    *   Reverses the order of a palette. e.g `-##Grayscale` is the ##Grayscale preset palette in reverse order (starts with white instead of black)
        
    
*   `**(start:end)**` - **Sub-palette**:
    
    *   Returns a portion of a palette. e.g `##Grayscale(1:8)` will return the first 8 blocks of the ##Grayscale preset palette.
        
    
*   `*****` - **Repeater**:
    
    *   Repeats the previous segment a given number of times. e.g `gold_block*10,diamond_block` will return a palette of 10 gold blocks, followed by a single diamond block.
        
    
*   `**[]**` - **Grouping**:
    
    *   Groups palettes together to allow a modifier to treat them as a single palette. e.g `-##Grayscale,gold_block` will return the ##Grayscale preset palette in reverse order, with a gold block at the end. Where `-[##Grayscale,gold_block]` will return the gold block at the start.
        
    
*   `**=**` - **Result**:
    
    *   Allows a palette to be tab-completed into its list of blocks if needed.
        
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/palettes/palettes-explained#video-tutorial)

Video Tutorial

[MegRae](https://megrae.art/)
 also made a tutorial for palettes:

[PreviousPermissions](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/getting-started/permissions)
[NextDefault Palettes](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/palettes/default-palettes)

Last updated 10 months ago

# Masks | ezEdits Wiki

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#aim)

`#aim`

#aim Mask[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#aim-mask)

`**#aim**` **or** `**#aim[True|False]**`

Takes the block the player is aiming at as the mask.

Optionally takes a True/False setting to make your aim sensitive to hitboxes.

*   False will treat all blocks as full blocks. E.g. you cannot `#aim` at the block behind a button.
    
*   True will respect the hitboxes of blocks you are looking at. E.g. you can `#aim` at the block behind a slab.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252FXu3BdYWJpNp475tYmV2p%252FaimMask.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dff6e57d5-ab08-4f01-b1ef-bdd297b0e861&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=be20cefc&sv=2)

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#attached)

`#attached`

#attached mask[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#attached-mask)

`**#attached[<vector,vector,vector ...>]**`

Masks to blocks which are attached to at least 1 adjacent non-air block.

Optionally takes a list of direction vectors to check instead of every side. e.g `#attached[up,down,left,north]`

In either case, attached means that the block is "touching" the adjacent block. So a bottom slab would not pass `#attached[up]` whereas a lantern with the state `[hanging=true]` would.

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#blocklight)

`#blocklight`

#blocklight Mask[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#blocklight-mask)

`**#blocklight[lightLevel]**` **or** `**#blocklight[minLevel][maxLevel]**`

Masks to blocks of a given block light (Illumination provided by light sources other than skylight). Optionally takes a minimum and maximum light level, matching any level within that range.

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#current)

`#current`

#current mask[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#current-mask)

Shorthand: `**#c**`

A mask which represents your current global mask (gmask).

e.g running `//gmask !#current` will invert your current gmask

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#eznoise)

`#eznoise`

#eznoise Mask[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#eznoise-mask)

`**#eznoisemask[noisePreset][<scale>][<threshold>][<seed>]**` **Alias:** `**#eznm**`

Uses a noise preset values `0.0-1.0` to match blocks above a given noise threshold.

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#fullblock)

`#fullblock`

#fullblock mask[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#fullblock-mask)

Masks to blocks which fill an entire cube space.

e.g 1-7 layers of snow will not pass, but 8 layers of snow, a block like stone, or a transparent block like glass will pass.

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#fuzzypalette)

`#fuzzypalette`

#fuzzypalette mask[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#fuzzypalette-mask)

`**#fuzzypalette[palette]**`

Shorthand: `**#fpalette**`

Masks to blocks which match any block in the palette, regardless of block data. Equivalent to `**#palette[palette][False]**`

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#infested)

`#infested`

#infested mask[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#infested-mask)

Masks to blocks which are infested with silverfish.

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#lightsource)

`#lightsource`

#lightsource Mask[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#lightsource-mask)

`**#lightsource**` **or** `**#lightsource[lightLevel]**` **or** `**#lightsource[minLevel][maxLevel]**`

Masks to blocks which emit light. Optionally takes a specific light level to match, or minimum and maximum light level, matching any level within that range.

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#near)

`#near`

#near Mask[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#near-mask)

`**#near[mask][distance]**` &#xNAN;`**#near[mask][minDistance][maxDistance]**` Masks to all blocks within a given spherical (Euclidean) distance of a mask. Doesn't modify blocks which match the inner `mask`. Can also be set to exclude blocks closer than the minimum distance.\\

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-7b11c225e5a5141a145413e65d76c6d0153a7b9e%252Fmask_near_mask.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ffee0971&sv=2) `**[mask]**`

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-98330380480b7cb3e45efeab1c3c6e0beeca3e39%252Fmask_near_max.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=98a41f2d&sv=2) `**[distance]**`

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-b3e146145c58602b7d0388806318bd8eb1c2341e%252Fmask_near_min_max.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=64f19af8&sv=2) `**[minDistance][maxDistance]**`

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#palette)

`#palette`

#palette mask[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#palette-mask)

`**#palette[palette][<strict>]**`

Masks to blocks which match any block in the palette.

Optional `<strict>` value of True or False to determine if block data must also match. e.g `oak_stairs[facing=east]` will only match with `oak_stairs[facing=west]` if strict is set to **False**.

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#truelight)

`#truelight`

#truelight Mask[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#truelight-mask)

`**#truelight[lightLevel]**` **or** `**#truelight[minLevel][maxLevel]**`

Masks to blocks of a given total light level (Illimunation provided by any light sources including skylight). Optionally takes a minimum and maximum light level, matching any level within that range.

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#vectorgradient)

`#vectorgradient`

#vectorgradient Mask[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks#vectorgradient-mask)

`**#vectorgradientmask[vector][distance][<noisePreset>][<noiseScale>][noiseSeed]**`

Shorthand: `#vgradientm`

Masks blocks along a vector with a given distance length. With closer blocks more likely to pass the mask check. Compatible with noise presets.

[PreviousNoise Commands](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/noise/noise-commands)
[NextPatterns](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/patterns)

# Noise Commands | ezEdits Wiki

All sub-commands are under `//eznoise` (`//ezn`) e.g `//eznoise list`

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/noise/noise-commands#eznoise)

`//eznoise ...`


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/noise/noise-commands#list-set)

`list [SET]`

*   `ALL` Lists all available noise presets
    
*   `DEFAULT` Lists all default plugin noise presets
    
*   `MINE` Lists all user-defined noise presets
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/noise/noise-commands#save-less-than-presetname-greater-than-less-than-noise-greater-than-f)

`save <presetName> <noise> [-f]`

Saves a user-defined noise preset with a given name. `-f` to override an existing noise preset.

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/noise/noise-commands#delete-less-than-presetname-greater-than)

`delete <presetName>`

Deletes a user-defined noise preset matching the given name.

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/noise/noise-commands#print-less-than-noise-greater-than)

`print <noise>`

Prints the settings of a given noise preset in chat.

[PreviousNoise Explained](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/noise/noise-explained)

# Superwand | ezEdits Wiki

The Super Wand tool offers four distinct modes for point selection and manipulation, providing an expanded way to work with region selections.

**WorldEditCUI is strongly recommended:** [**https://modrinth.com/mod/worldedit-cui**](https://modrinth.com/mod/worldedit-cui)

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/superwand#modes)

Modes

1.  **TRACE Mode**: Selects the block you are targeting.
    
2.  **POSITION Mode**: Selects the block at your current player position.
    
3.  **RELATIVE Mode**: Selects a point relative to the last point placed and the player's aim direction.
    
4.  **GRAB Mode**: Enables grabbing and moving a point or the entire selection.
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/superwand#controls)

Controls

*   **Right Click**:
    
    *   In point selection modes, selects a new point or replaces the most recent point if the selection is full.
        
    *   In GRAB mode, picks up a point or the entire selection, moving it with the player's movements.
        
    
*   **Left Click**:
    
    *   In point selection modes, removes the last set point.
        
    *   In GRAB mode, drops the point or selection.
        
    
*   **Sneak + Left Click**: Cycles through the tool modes.
    
*   **Swap Hand (Default F Key)**: Reverses the order of points in the selection.
    
*   **Sneak + Swap Hand (Default F Key)**: Shifts all convex selection points along by one position in the list of points.
    

[PreviousPlacement Brushes](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/brushes/placement-brushes)
[NextSmoothblocks](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/smoothblocks/smoothblocks)

Last updated 11 months ago

*   [Modes](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/superwand#modes)
    
*   [Controls](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/superwand#controls)

# Patterns | ezEdits Wiki

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/patterns#aim)

`#aim`

#aim Pattern[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/patterns#aim-pattern)

`**#aim**` **or** `**#aim[True|False]**`

Takes the block the player is aiming at as the Pattern.

Optionally takes a True/False setting to make your aim sensitive to hitboxes.

*   False will treat all blocks as full blocks. E.g. you cannot `#aim` at the block behind a button.
    
*   True will respect the hitboxes of blocks you are looking at. E.g. you can `#aim` at the block behind a slab.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252F699IOaviExrmZAuGj2GW%252FaimPattern.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D90f847f0-c517-45b4-9391-01f8c0d0bf6c&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d8f04aab&sv=2)

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/patterns#eznoise)

`#eznoise`

#eznoise Pattern[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/patterns#eznoise-pattern)

`**#eznoisepattern[palette][noisePreset][<scale>][<seed>]**` **Alias:** `**#eznp**`

Uses a noise preset values to return palette blocks. **Which also has the following in-built presets:**

*   `**#ridged[palette][<scale>][<seed>]**`
    
*   `**#smoothcells[palette][<scale>][<seed>]**`
    
*   `**#voronoiedge[palette][<scale>][<seed>]**`
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/patterns#palette)

`#palette`

#palette Pattern[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/patterns#palette-pattern)

`**#palette[palette]**`

Takes the given palette and returns a list of palette blocks. Can be used as a random block pattern.

e.g. `//set #palette[##ice]` is the same as `//set [blue_ice,packed_ice,ice]`

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/patterns#selection)

`#selection`

#selection Pattern[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/patterns#selection-pattern)

`**#selection[selection][<offset>]**`

Shorthand: `**#sel[selection][<offset>]**`

Sets blocks using the blocks currently in world at the location of the saved selection. Acts as if the selection were tiled/stacked.

Optional `<offset>` variable to offset the pattern by a given vector.

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/patterns#vectorgradient)

`#vectorgradient`

#vectorgradient Pattern[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/patterns#vectorgradient-pattern)

`**#vectorgradientpattern[palette][vector][distance][<noisePreset>][<noiseScale>][<noiseSeed>]**` **Alias:** `**#vgradientp**`

Sets palette blocks along a vector with a given distance length with the block chosen based on distance plus a blending factor. Can also use noise presets.

[PreviousMasks](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/masks-and-patterns/masks)
[NextBrushes](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/brushes)

# Region | ezEdits Wiki

A miscellaneous collection of commands which operate within your selected region.

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/region#ezvines)

`//ezvines`

Vines[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/region#vines)

`**//ezvines <mask> <pattern> [percentage] [min_length] [max_length]**`

`**Alias: //vines**`

*   **Mask**: Specifies the mask matching blocks to hang "vines" from.
    
*   **Pattern**: Determines the pattern of blocks to place.
    
*   **Percentage** (Default: 10%): Sets the percentage of blocks to hang vines from.
    
*   **Min Length** (Default: 2): Specifies the minimum vine length.
    
*   **Max Length** (Default: 5): Defines the maximum vine length.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-7e29c93a8161de7126bcb90a3bc035143b17ef19%252Fezvines_mask.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e5e1db8b&sv=2) `**<mask>**`

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-09aa944db5aa745b1ee554c51ab9bd233816b953%252Fezvines_percentage.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a571d60e&sv=2) `**[percentage]**`

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-11932cbd23cc73e161ace8ac55eeb6bbf790c0c3%252Fezvines_length.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=de39ec66&sv=2) `**[min_length] [max_length]**`

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/region#ezmoss)

`//ezmoss`

Moss[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/region#moss)

`**//ezmoss <pattern> [amount] [smooth_radii] [smooth_iterations]**`

`**Alias: //moss**`

*   **Pattern**: Determines the block pattern to use for the moss.
    
*   **Amount** (Default: 2.0): Specifies the amount of moss to place. Decimal values are allowed, and values are somewhat arbitrary.
    
*   **Smooth Radii** (Default: 1): Sets the smoothing radii for the moss placement. Can be one radius or three comma-separated radii, in the order of East/West, Up/Down, North/South.
    
*   **Smooth Iterations** (Default: 5): Defines the number of smoothing iterations to apply.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-3c0dd0b0ec0bd89769e92bc2bada8fc72319c580%252Fezmoss_amount.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=34bcdd79&sv=2) `**[amount]**`

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-ace4ae0505d8fcb53bea1c77dd797c22637e0f30%252Fezmoss_radius.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9a044a8&sv=2) `**[smooth_radii]**`

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-233fbdb078d01912de556ad5a36e5eab754b4043%252Fezmoss_radii.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7b9e39b&sv=2) `**[smooth_radii]**`

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-78e0b380dfaf8e960cc4d0beaf8f1a6d589a39ae%252Fezmoss_iterations.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5b3a3699&sv=2) `**[smooth_iterations]**`

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/region#ezslabmerge)

`//ezslabmerge`

SlabMerge[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/region#slabmerge)

`**//ezslabmerge <mask> [-b] [-t]**`

`**Alias: //slabmerge**`

*   **Mask**: Specifies the mask to select which blocks to affect within the region.
    
*   **\-b**: When used, will also convert bottom slabs to full blocks.
    
*   **\-t**: When used, will also convert top slabs to full blocks.
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/region#ezstatecyle)

`//ezstatecyle`

StateCycle[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/region#statecycle)

`**//ezstatecycle <mask> <state>**`

`**Alias: //statecycle**`

*   **Mask**: Specifies the mask to select which blocks to affect within the region.
    
*   **State**: Identifies the block state value to cycle through for each block in the selection.

# Palette Gradient Brushes | ezEdits Wiki

The following commands feature brushes for creating gradients.

* * *

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/brushes/palette-gradient-brushes#ezbr-gradient)

`//ezbr` `gradient`

Gradient Brush[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/brushes/palette-gradient-brushes#gradient-brush)

`**//ezbr gradient``**` `**<palette> [radius] [interpolation] [bleed] [-avw] [-n <noise>] [-z <scale>] [-d <distanceFunction>]**`

The `gradient` brush allows you to first define a plane by selecting 2 points, you can then paint with your gradient with blocks chosen based on distance along this plane.

**Left Click** **to start a plane at your target block** **Sneak + Left Click** **to start a plane at the player position** **Right Click** **to set the end of the plane at your target block OR paint palette blocks if the plane is set** **Sneak + Right Click** **to set the end of the plane at the player position OR paint palette blocks if the plane is set** **Swap Hands** **(Default F key) to toggle between GLOBAL and PER\_ITEM active gradients**

*   **Palette**: Specifies the palette to use for the gradient.
    
*   **Radius** (Default: 8): Sets the radius of the brush.
    
*   **Interpolation** (Default: NONE): Determines the type of interpolation used in the gradient transition.
    
*   **Bleed** (Default: 0.5): Adjusts the strength of interpolation, with a normal range from 0 to 1.
    
*   `**-a**`: When activated, the gradient is allowed to replace air blocks.
    
*   `**-v**`: Deactivates WorldEditCUI integration.
    
*   `-w`: Try to texture shaping blocks (slabs, stairs, etc.) with the closest existing material.
    
*   `**-n <noise>**` (Default: `White()`): Adds an underlying noise field to the gradient effect.
    
*   `**-z <scale>**` (Default: 1): Modifies the scale of the noise.
    
*   `**-d <distanceFunction>**` (Default: NONE): Sets the distance mode changing the brush to work based on distance from the initial block with the given distance function.
    

* * *

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/brushes/palette-gradient-brushes#ezbr-gradientstroke)

`//ezbr` `gradientstroke`

Gradient Stroke Brush[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/brushes/palette-gradient-brushes#gradient-stroke-brush)

`**//ezbr gradientstroke``**` `**<palette> [radius] [interpolation] [bleed] [-advwx] [-n <noise>] [-z <scale>]**`

The `gradientstroke` brush allows for gradient application along a path (stroke) defined by selecting points.

**Left Click** **to add points** **Sneak + Left Click** **to remove the last point** **Right Click** **to confirm & place the gradient stroke** **Sneak + Right Click** **to clear all points** **Swap Hands** **(Default F key) to toggle between GLOBAL and PER\_ITEM active gradients**

*   **Palette**: Specifies the block pattern for the gradient.
    
*   **Radius** (Default: 8): Sets the radius of the brush.
    
*   **Interpolation** (Default: LINEAR): Determines the type of interpolation used in the gradient transition.
    
*   **Bleed** (Default: 0.5): Adjusts the strength of interpolation, with a normal range from 0 to 1.
    
*   `**-a**`: When activated, allows the gradient to replace air blocks.
    
*   `**-d**`: Activates the 'distance to center' mode which applies the gradient based on distance to the middle of the stroke line instead of distance along the stroke.
    
*   `**-v**`: Deactivates WorldEditCUI integration.
    
*   `-w`: Try to texture shaping blocks (slabs, stairs, etc.) with the closest existing material.
    
*   `**-x**`: Clears the brush's path after every placed stroke.
    
*   `**-n <noise>**` (Default: `White()`): Adds an underlying noise field to the gradient effect.
    
*   `**-z <scale>**` (Default: 1): Modifies the scale of the noise.
    

* * *

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/brushes/palette-gradient-brushes#gradient-parameters)

Gradient Parameters


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are a few parameters to creating a gradient worth explaining.

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/brushes/palette-gradient-brushes#bleed)

Bleed

First off, the `**bleed**` parameter.

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-40f5cd90087ef2c78c423a54a913acf342d73409%252FGradientInterpolationTapered2.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=17530eec&sv=2)

The bleed parameter determines how much the colors bleed into each other.

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/brushes/palette-gradient-brushes#noise)

Noise

The pattern of how this bleeding takes place can be determined by `**noise**`. The GIF above was using White noise (`-n White`), while the following GIFs use Perlin noise (`-n Perlin(Freq:0.25)`)

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-fdb3525cd7358d4e62d4efe1dddecf6e0fe05987%252FGradientInterpolationTapered.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9105583f&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/brushes/palette-gradient-brushes#you-can-also-put-in-any-noise.-here-are-a-few-more-examples)

You can also put in any noise. Here are a few more examples:

`**-n Perlin(Freq:0.25)**`

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-db7124c532f5bc8b6ac27ce537bf833603a4f0c2%252FGradientInterpolationNoise_example1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7f8cb715&sv=2)

`**-n Cellular(Freq:0.15)**`

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-1e90108b272026438da4ca5deb82b4eb66d5d25b%252FGradientInterpolationNoise_example3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e984ac7d&sv=2)

`**-n @@ridged(Freq:0.15)**`

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-c4e5f3af1e103f4816a2fe7d4e23fc36001667e9%252FGradientInterpolationNoise_example2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b3ebc845&sv=2)

`**-n Shard(Freq:0.15)**`

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-3fac181f3493c0b04b73a02e521faa71bf6e0565%252FGradientInterpolationNoise_example4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f36f97be&sv=2)

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/brushes/palette-gradient-brushes#interpolation-mode)

Interpolation Mode

In the following, we compare the five different `**interpolation modes**` of applying the noise to the gradient. The GIFs go through increasing and decreasing bleed values between 0 and 1.

_The blue square's top and bottom show where the gradient starts and ends_

#### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/brushes/palette-gradient-brushes#none)

NONE

No interpolation is applied.

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-212859f5d6836ea4ab56e5362efc9ba1bf002f27%252FGradientInterpolationNone.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=28467761&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/brushes/palette-gradient-brushes#linear)

LINEAR

The noise is applied with a constant factor throughout the entire gradient. Because of that, the gradient is "clipping" outside our two selected positions.

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-540e522c65bb95d7a11eaa8c860936b18e63abbe%252FGradientInterpolationLinear.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8976659b&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/brushes/palette-gradient-brushes#tapered)

TAPERED

Applies the noise strongest in the middle of the gradient and tapers off towards the start and end to avoid "clipping" outside of the given positions.

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-fdb3525cd7358d4e62d4efe1dddecf6e0fe05987%252FGradientInterpolationTapered.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9105583f&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/brushes/palette-gradient-brushes#bezier)

BEZIER

Uses Bezier interpolation to apply the noise more softly and smoothly. Breaks for a bleed value of >1.

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-df1ee0f1842fc60c7bb61c815d93eb44df4dc747%252FGradientInterpolationBezier.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dec2f660&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/brushes/palette-gradient-brushes#sin)

SIN

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-71de92f790b03175e64fb1af992baf48c841ddd1%252FGradientInterpolationSin.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8228ac13&sv=2)

[NextPlacement Brushes](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/brushes-and-tools/brushes/placement-brushes)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Survival | ezEdits Wiki

All sub-commands are under `//ezsurvival` (`//ezsv`) e.g `//ezsv deinfest`

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/survival#ezsurvival)

`//ezsurvival ...`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/survival#deinfest)

`deinfest`

`**//ezsv deinfest**`

Replaces infested blocks with their non-infested counterpart. For example, `infested_stone` will become `stone`

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/survival#persist)

`persist`

`**//ezsv persist [ON|OFF]**`

Toggles leaf block persistence on or off. Having persistence on prevents leaf decay.

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/survival#wax)

`wax`

`**//ezsv wax [ON|OFF]**`

Toggles waxing of copper blocks and signs on or off. Waxing copper blocks prevents them changing states due to age. Waxing signs prevents them from being edited.

[PreviousSurface](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/surface)
[NextTexturing](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/texturing)

# Noisegen | ezEdits Wiki

All sub-commands are under `//eznoisegen` (`//noisegen`, `//ng`) e.g `//ng heightmap`

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/noisegen#eznoisegen)

`//eznoisegen ...`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/noisegen#heightmap)

heightmap

Heightmap (2D)[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/noisegen#heightmap-2d)

`**//eznoisegen heightmap <palette> <noise> [height] [-z <zoom>] [-s <seed>] [-o <offset>] [-ct]**`

*   **Palette**: Specifies the palette of blocks to use.
    
*   **Noise**: Defines the noise preset to use.
    
*   **Height** (Default: 0): Controls the height from the bottom of your selection. A value of 0 will take the selection's height. _Can place blocks above the selection if the height is great enough_
    
*   **\-z** (Default: 1): Adjusts the zoom level of the noise.
    
*   **\-s** (Default: -1): Sets the noise seed.
    
*   **\-o** (Default: (0,0,0)): Offsets the noise generation coordinates by a given vector (X,Y,Z).
    
*   **\-c**: When used, centres the noise generation on the world coordinates of the selection.
    
*   **\-t**: Enables smooth mode, specifically for snow, water, and lava blocks in the palette \[Applicable only in heightmap mode\].
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/noisegen#terrain)

terrain

Terrain (3D)[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/noisegen#terrain-3d)

`**//eznoisegen terrain <palette> <noise> [height] [strength] [-z <scale>] [-s <seed>] [-l <smear>] [-o <offset>] [-c]**`

*   **Palette**: Specifies the palette of blocks to use.
    
*   **Noise**: Defines the noise preset to use.
    
*   **Height** (Default: 0): Controls the height from the bottom of your selection. A value of 0 will take the selection's height. _Can place blocks above the selection if the height is great enough_
    
*   **Strength** (Default: 1,0.5,0): Takes up to 3 comma-separated values which controls the strength of noise at various heights:
    
    *   `_0.5_` _would be 50% strength everywhere_
        
    *   `_0.7,0_` _would be 70% strength at the very bottom and 0% at the top, with everything in-between being a smooth transition_
        
    *   `_0,1,0_` _would be 0% strength at the bottom, 100% in the middle, and 0% at the top_
        
    
*   **\-z** (Default: 1): Adjusts the zoom level of the noise.
    
*   **\-s** (Default: -1): Sets the noise seed.
    
*   **\-l** (Default: 0): Applies a vertical smear to 3D noise.
    
*   **\-o** (Default: (0,0,0)): Offsets the noise generation coordinates by a given vector (X,Y,Z).
    
*   **\-c**: When used, centres the noise generation on the world coordinates of the selection.
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/noisegen#advanced)

advanced

Advanced[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/noisegen#advanced-1)

`**//eznoisegen <palette> <noise> [lowerThreshold] [upperThreshold] [-z <scale>] [-s <seed>] [-l <smear>] [-o <offset>] [-chnt]**`

*   **Palette**: Specifies the palette of blocks to use.
    
*   **Noise**: Defines the noise preset to use.
    
*   **Lower Threshold** (Default: 0): Sets the lower threshold for noise generation, with support for WorldEdit expressions (range: 0-1.0).
    
*   **Upper Threshold** (Default: 0.5): Sets the upper threshold for noise generation, with support for WorldEdit expressions (range: 0-1.0).
    
*   **\-z** (Default: 1): Adjusts the zoom level of the noise.
    
*   **\-s** (Default: -1): Sets the noise seed.
    
*   **\-l** (Default: 0): Applies a vertical smear to 3D noise.
    
*   **\-o** (Default: (0,0,0)): Offsets the noise generation coordinates by a given vector (X,Y,Z).
    
*   **\-c**: When used, centres the noise generation on the world coordinates of the selection.
    
*   **\-h**: Activates heightmap mode using 2D noise. &#xNAN;_Heightmap mode is only compatible with Cuboid, Cylinder, or Polygon region types._
    
*   **\-n**: Uses normalized (-1 to 1) selection-centred coordinates for noise generation.
    
*   **\-t**: Enables smooth mode, specifically for snow, water, and lava blocks in the palette \[Applicable only in heightmap mode\].
    

[PreviousFlowfields](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/flowfields)
[NextRegion](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/region)

Last updated 11 months ago

*   [//eznoisegen ...](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/noisegen#eznoisegen)
    
*   [heightmap](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/noisegen#heightmap)
    
*   [terrain](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/noisegen#terrain)
    
*   [advanced](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/noisegen#advanced)

# Stained Glass | ezEdits Wiki

Commands related to using stained glass for color.

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/stained-glass#ezstainedglassgradient)

`//ezstainedglassgradient`

Glass Gradient[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/stained-glass#glass-gradient)

`**//ezstainedglassgradient <startColor> [endColor] <layers> [length] [quality] [direction] [-c <backgroundColor>] [-bs]**`

`**Aliases: //stainedglassgradient, //glassgradient**`

*   **StartColor**: Specifies the starting color (as a Hex code) for the gradient.
    
*   **EndColor** (Default: None): Specifies the end color (as a Hex code) for the gradient. If no value is provided, then the start color will be used for the whole gradient.
    
*   **Layers**: How many layers of glass to use in creating the gradient.
    
*   **Length** (Default: 1): How many blocks long should the gradient be.
    
*   **Quality** (Default: 7): How accurate should the gradient be. A higher value may take longer to run.
    
*   **\-c** (Default: #000000): Specifies the background colour (as a Hex code) that the gradient is on if **\-b** flag is not used.
    
*   **\-b**: Finds the closest solid block to place behind the glass to increase color accuracy. This is much more resource intensive.
    
*   **\-s**: Skip duplicate layer combinations.
    

[PreviousAdvanced Spline Shapes](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/spline/advanced-spline-shapes)
[NextSurface](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/surface)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Smoothing | ezEdits Wiki

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/smoothing#ezsmooth)

`//ezsmooth`

Smooth[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/smoothing#smooth)

`**//ezsmooth <radii> <iterations> <bias> [-w <profile>]**`

`**Alias: //ezsm**`

The `//ezsmooth` command smooths the edges and surfaces of a selected region using a 3 dimensional smoothing algorithm.

*   **Radii**: The smoothing radius or radii, which can be a single value or three comma-separated values for the East/West, Up/Down, and North/South directions, respectively. This parameter controls the extent of the smoothing effect.
    
*   **Iterations**: The number of times the smoothing operation is executed. More iterations lead to a smoother outcome but increase processing time.
    
*   **Bias**: A value between -1.0 and 1.0 that adjusts the smoothing effect's expansion or contraction. Positive values expand the smoothed area, while negative values contract it.
    
*   **\-w**: See [Smoothblocks](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/smoothblocks/smoothblocks)
    .
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/smoothing#ezinflate)

`//ezinflate`

Inflate[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/smoothing#inflate)

`**//ezinflate <radii> [-w <profile>]**`

`**Alias: //inflate**`

The `//ezinflate` command expands the volume of blocks within a selected region by a specified amount, effectively "inflating" the build.

*   **Radii**: Specifies the expansion distance, which can be a single value or three comma-separated values for the East/West, Up/Down, and North/South directions, respectively. This value determines how far from the original surfaces the new, inflated surfaces will be created.
    
*   **\-w**: See [Smoothblocks](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/smoothblocks/smoothblocks)
    .
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/smoothing#ezdeflate)

`//ezdeflate`

Deflate[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/smoothing#deflate)

`**//ezdeflate <radii> [-w <profile>]**`

`**Alias: //deflate**`

The `//ezdeflate` command contracts the volume of blocks within a selected region by a specified amount, effectively "deflating" the build.

*   **Radii**: Specifies the expansion distance, which can be a single value or three comma-separated values for the East/West, Up/Down, and North/South directions, respectively. This value determines how far inwards from the original surfaces that blocks will be removed.
    
*   **\-w**: See [Smoothblocks](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/smoothblocks/smoothblocks)
    .
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/smoothing#ezsmoothblocks-v0.15.0-and-above)

`//ezsmoothblocks` (v0.15.0 and above)

Smooth Blocks[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/smoothing#smooth-blocks)

`**//ezsmoothblocks <profile> <radius> <bias>**`

`**Alias: //ezsb**`

The `//ezsmoothblocks` command modifies a selected region by placing slabs, stairs, and walls to create a significantly smoother surface.

*   **Profile**: Determines the set of shaping blocks used. See [Profiles](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/smoothblocks/smoothblocks#profiles)
    .
    

*   **Radius**: Specifies the smoothing radius in blocks. This value determines the area around each block that is considered during the smoothing process. The larger the value to more aggressive the smoothing.
    

*   **Bias**: A value between -1.0 and 1.0 that adjusts the smoothing effect which determines how many blocks are added or removed. Positive values will lead to more blocks being placed than removed, while negative values will remove more blocks than add.
    
*   **\-w**: See [Smoothblocks](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/smoothblocks/smoothblocks)
    .
    

#### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/smoothing#ezsmoothblocks-v0.14.0-and-older)

`//ezsmoothblocks` (v0.14.0 and older)

Smooth Blocks (Legacy)[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/smoothing#smooth-blocks-legacy)

`**//ezsmoothblocks <radius> <iterations> <bias> [-s] [-t] [-w]**`

`**Alias: //smoothblocks**`

The `//ezsmoothblocks` command modifies a selected region by placing slabs, stairs, and walls to create a significantly smoother surface.

*   **Radius**: Specifies the smoothing radius in blocks. This value determines the area around each block that is considered during the smoothing process.
    
*   **Iterations**: The number of times the smoothing operation is executed. More iterations result in a smoother outcome but increase processing time.
    
*   **Bias**: A value between -1.0 and 1.0 that adjusts the smoothing effect's expansion or contraction. Positive values tend to expand the smoothed area, while negative values contract it, offering control over the final appearance.
    
*   **\-s**: Limits the smoothing process to only use slabs.
    
*   **\-t**: Excludes walls from smoothing.
    
*   **\-w**: Uses an alternative set of blocks.
    

* * *

[PreviousShapes](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/shapes)
[NextSpline](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/spline)

Last updated 2 months ago

*   [//ezsmooth](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/smoothing#ezsmooth)
    
*   [//ezinflate](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/smoothing#ezinflate)
    
*   [//ezdeflate](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/smoothing#ezdeflate)
    
*   [//ezsmoothblocks (v0.15.0 and above)](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/smoothing#ezsmoothblocks-v0.15.0-and-above)

# Shapes | ezEdits Wiki

All sub-commands are under `//ezshapes` (`//ezsh`) e.g `//ezshapes polydome`

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/shapes#ezshapes)

`//ezshapes ...`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/shapes#cone)

`cone`

Cone[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/shapes#cone-1)

`**//ezsh cone <pattern> <radii> <height> [rotation] [-dhos]**`

*   **Pattern**: Specifies the block pattern.
    
*   **Radii**: Defines the radii of the cone. The first value is for the North/South direction, and the second is for East/West. These directions can change if the cone is rotated.
    
*   **Height**: Sets the height of the cone.
    
*   **Rotation** (Default: 0): Determines the angle of rotation about the y-axis, in degrees. This can be aligned with the player's aiming direction if the `-o` switch is used.
    
*   **\-d**: When activated, generates the cone with the pointy side facing downwards.
    
*   **\-h**: Makes a hollow shape.
    
*   **\-o**: When used, the player's aim direction is considered for the cone's rotation.
    
*   **\-s**: When used, the players selection will be moved to roughly cover the shape
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/shapes#polydome)

`polydome`

Polydome[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/shapes#polydome-1)

`**//ezsh polydome <pattern> <sides> <radius> <height> [-vs]**`

*   **Pattern**: Specifies the block pattern.
    
*   **Sides**: Defines the number of sides for the polydome.
    
*   **Radius**: Sets the radius of the polydome.
    
*   **Height** (Default: 1): Determines the height of the dome.
    
*   **\-v**: Specifies a vertex pattern, altering the appearance at the vertices of the polydome.
    
*   **\-s**: When used, the players selection will be moved to roughly cover the shape
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/shapes#polygon)

`polygon`

Polygon[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/shapes#polygon-1)

`**//ezsh polygon <pattern> <sides> <radius> <height> [direction] [-s]**`

*   **Pattern**: Specifies the block pattern.
    
*   **Sides**: Defines the number of sides for the polygon.
    
*   **Radius**: Sets the radius of the polygon.
    
*   **Height** (Default: 1): Determines the height of the polygon.
    
*   **Direction** (Default: Player AIM): Specifies the direction of placement, which can include diagonals.
    
*   **\-s**: When used, the players selection will be moved to roughly cover the shape
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/shapes#square)

`square`

Square[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/shapes#square-1)

`**//ezsh square <pattern> <radius> <height> [-fws]**`

*   **Pattern**: Specifies the block pattern.
    
*   **Radius**: Sets the radius of the square.
    
*   **Height** (Default: 1): Determines the height of the square.
    
*   **\-f**: When activated, only the faces of the square are generated.
    
*   **\-w**: When used, only the walls of the square are generated.
    
*   **\-s**: When used, the players selection will be moved to roughly cover the shape
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/shapes#tetrahedron)

`tetrahedron`

Tetrahedron[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/shapes#tetrahedron-1)

`**//ezsh tetrahedron <pattern> <radius> [rotation] [-hos]**`

*   **Pattern**: Specifies the block pattern.
    
*   **Radius**: Sets the size of the Tetrahedron.
    
*   **Rotation** (Default: 0): Determines the angle of rotation about the y-axis, in degrees. This can be aligned with the player's aiming direction if the -o switch is used.
    
*   **\-h**: Makes a hollow shape.
    
*   **\-o**: When used, the player's aim direction is considered for the Tetrahedron's rotation.
    
*   **\-s**: When used, the players selection will be moved to roughly cover the shape
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/shapes#torus)

`torus`

Torus[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/shapes#torus-1)

`**//ezsh torus <pattern> <major_radius> <minor_radius> <cross_section> [-hos]**`

*   **Pattern**: Specifies the block pattern.
    
*   **Major Radius**: Sets the major radius of the torus.
    
*   **Minor Radius**: Sets the minor radius of the torus.
    
*   **Cross Section**: Determines the cross section shape of the torus:
    
    *   `CIRCLE`
        
    *   `DIAMOND`
        
    *   `ROUNDED_SQUARE`
        
    *   `SQUARE`
        
    
*   **\-h**: Makes a hollow shape.
    
*   **\-o**: When used, the rotation of the torus aligns with the player's aiming direction
    
*   **\-s**: When used, the players selection will be moved to roughly cover the shape
    

[PreviousSelections](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/selections)
[NextSmoothing](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/smoothing)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [//ezshapes ...](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/shapes#ezshapes)
    
*   [cone](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/shapes#cone)
    
*   [polydome](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/shapes#polydome)
    
*   [polygon](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/shapes#polygon)
