# Spline | ezEdits Wiki

Video tutorial by [eztaK](https://linktr.ee/eztak)

ezEdits provides an extensive interface to place and embed various shapes and structures along a 1-dimensional interpolated path in 3-D space.

The paths are defined by WorldEdits convex selections (`//sel convex`). When using a cuboid selection, the spline will be a direct line from pos1 to pos2.

All sub-commands are under `**//ezspline**` The abbreviation/alias of it is `**//ezsp**`

* * *

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/spline#subpage-overview)

Subpage Overview


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [**Common Parameters**](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/spline/common-parameters)
    
    *   covers all arguments and flags that are available to **all** `ezspline` subcommands. These are:
        
        *   [`<radii>`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/spline/common-parameters#radii)
            
        *   [`[-p <kbParameters>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/spline/common-parameters#kb-parameters)
            
        *   [`[-q <quality>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/spline/common-parameters#quality)
            
        *   [`[-r <startingRoll>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/spline/common-parameters#roll)
            
        *   [`[-s <stretchFactor>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/spline/common-parameters#stretch)
            
        *   [`[-t <twistAngle>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/spline/common-parameters#twist)

# Smoothing | French | ezEdits Wiki

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/smoothing#ezsmooth)

`//ezsmooth`

Smooth[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/smoothing#smooth)

`**//ezsmooth <radii> <iterations> <bias>**`

`**Alias: //ezsm**`

La `//ezsmooth` commande lisse les bords et les surfaces d'une région sélectionnée à l'aide d'un algorithme de lissage tridimensionnel.

*   **Radii**: le ou les rayons de lissage, qui peuvent être une valeur unique ou trois valeurs séparées par des virgules pour les directions Est/Ouest, Haut/Bas et Nord/Sud, respectivement. Ce paramètre contrôle l'étendue de l'effet de lissage.
    
*   **Iterations**: nombre de fois que l'opération de lissage est exécutée. Un nombre plus élevé d'itérations conduit à un résultat plus fluide mais augmente le temps de traitement.
    
*   **Bias**: valeur comprise entre -1,0 et 1,0 qui ajuste l'expansion ou la contraction de l'effet de lissage. Les valeurs positives élargissent la zone lissée, tandis que les valeurs négatives la contractent.
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/smoothing#ezinflate)

`//ezinflate`

Inflate[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/smoothing#inflate)

`**//ezinflate <radius>**`

`**Alias: //inflate**`

La `//ezinflate` commande augmente le volume des blocs dans une région sélectionnée d'une quantité spécifiée, « gonflant » ainsi efficacement la construction.

*   **Radius**: Spécifie la distance d'expansion en blocs. Cette valeur détermine à quelle distance des surfaces d'origine les nouvelles surfaces gonflées seront créées.
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/smoothing#ezdeflate)

`//ezdeflate`

Deflate[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/smoothing#deflate)

`**//ezdeflate <radius>**`

`**Alias: //deflate**`

La `//ezdeflate` commande contracte le volume des blocs dans une région sélectionnée d'une quantité spécifiée, « dégonflant » ainsi efficacement la construction.

*   **Radius**: spécifie la distance d'expansion en blocs. Cette valeur détermine la distance à laquelle les blocs seront supprimés à partir des surfaces d'origine.
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/smoothing#ezsmoothblocks)

`//ezsmoothblocks`

Smooth Blocks[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/smoothing#smooth-blocks)

`**//ezsmoothblocks <radius> <iterations> <bias> [-s] [-t] [-w]**`

`**Alias: //smoothblocks**`

La `//ezsmoothblocks` commande modifie une région sélectionnée en plaçant des dalles, des escaliers et des murs pour créer une surface nettement plus lisse.

*   **Radius**: spécifie le rayon de lissage en blocs. Cette valeur détermine la zone autour de chaque bloc qui est prise en compte pendant le processus de lissage.
    
*   **Iterations**:nombre de fois que l'opération de lissage est exécutée. Un nombre plus élevé d'itérations produit un résultat plus lisse, mais augmente le temps de traitement.
    
*   **Bias**: valeur comprise entre -1,0 et 1,0 qui ajuste l'expansion ou la contraction de l'effet de lissage. Les valeurs positives tendent à élargir la zone lissée, tandis que les valeurs négatives la contractent, offrant ainsi un contrôle sur l'apparence finale.
    
*   **\-s**: limite le processus de lissage pour n'utiliser que des dalles.
    
*   **\-t**: exclut les murs du lissage.
    
*   **\-w**: utilise un ensemble alternatif de blocs.
    

[PreviousForme](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/shapes)
[NextSpline](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/spline)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [//ezsmooth](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/smoothing#ezsmooth)
    
*   [//ezinflate](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/smoothing#ezinflate)
    
*   [//ezdeflate](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/smoothing#ezdeflate)

# ezEdits Docs | Chinese | ezEdits Wiki

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2203755917-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FprArdPVTMFbs2Ewnf2OB%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-1da2f8d7bf5194f050fb262614f92683eab677d7%252Flogofinal5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fac8a5fd&sv=2)

什么是 ezEdits？


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

ezEdits 是一个 WorldEdit/FastAsyncWorldEdit (WE/FAWE) 扩展插件，它增加了众多新命令、图案、蒙板和工具，帮助您创作出令人惊叹的作品！

# Flowfields | French | ezEdits Wiki

Commandes basées sur le concept de « champs de flux », souvent observés dans l'art génératif.

Conceptuellement, ils utilisent une fonction (du bruit dans notre cas) pour générer un ensemble de vecteurs le long d'une grille, ou d'un champ, qui dictera la manière dont les particules circulent à travers ce champ.

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/flowfields#ezflowfield)

`//ezflowfield`

Flow Field[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/flowfields#flow-field)

`**//ezflowfield <palette> <lines> <iterations> <velocity> <paletteScalar> <noise> [-m <source>] [-h <distributionMode>] [-i <inertia>] [-g <gravity>] [-j <jitter>] [-b <boundary>] [-x <xMod>] [-y <yMod>] [-z <zMod>] [-p <progression>] [-s <seed>] [-c] [-f] [-t]**`

`**Alias: //flow**`

Génère un champ de flux dans une sélection, créant un motif dynamique basé sur les nombreux paramètres disponibles.

*   **Palette**: Spécifie la palette de blocs à utiliser pour générer le champ de flux.
    
*   **ligne**: définit le nombre de lignes ou une distribution en pourcentage pour déterminer la densité de remplissage du champ de flux dans la sélection. Par exemple, `100` générera 100 lignes, `100%` générera 1 ligne pour chaque bloc de la région.
    
*   **Iterations** (par défaut: 32): le nombre d'itérations ou d'étapes par ligne contrôlant leur durée.
    
*   **Velocity** (par défaut: 1): la vitesse à laquelle les points se déplacent sur la surface.
    
*   **PaletteScalar** (par défaut: 1.0): met à l'échelle la valeur utilisée pour sélectionner un bloc de palette.
    
*   **Noise** (par défaut: `Perlin()`): le type de noise utilisé pour générer le champ de flux.
    
*   **\-m**: Applique un masque pour limiter les points de départ du flux, en concentrant l'effet sur des zones spécifiques.
    
*   **\-h**: Active le mode heightmap pour créer des champs de flux 2D, avec des modes de distribution de blocs facultatifs.
    
*   **\-i** (par défaut: 0.0): définit la pondération d'inertie du flux, contrôlant dans quelle mesure les directions de mouvement précédentes influencent la suivante.
    
*   **\-g** (par défaut: (0,0,0) ): applique la gravité aux points, les tirant dans la direction spécifiée.
    
*   **\-j** (par défaut: (0,0,0) ): ajoute de la gigue aux points de départ des lignes. Utile avec `-m` l'indicateur.
    
*   **\-b** (par défaut: 0): étend la limite de calcul sans placer de blocs en dehors de la sélection d'origine. Ne place pas de blocs en dehors de la sélection.
    
*   **\-x, -y, -z**: modifie les coordonnées du flux, permettant des transformations telles que la mise à l'échelle ou la rotation. Prend une expression WorldEdit, Par exemple, `-x *10`pour multiplier l'axe des x par 10.
    
*   **\-p** (par défaut: 1:1): ajuste la force de la ligne au fur et à mesure de sa progression, accepte des valeurs négatives pour démarrer ou terminer sur une force de point qui se soustrait au champ de flux.
    
*   **\-s** (par défaut: -1): remplace la valeur de noise par défaut.
    
*   **\-c**: Renvoie la boucle du champ.
    
*   **\-f**: Remplit les espaces avec le bloc le plus bas de la palette.
    
*   **\-t**: génère un champ d'écoulement 3D à la place. La génération peut nécessiter beaucoup de temps.
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/flowfields#ezflowline)

`//ezflowline`

Flow Line[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/flowfields#flow-line)

`**/ezflowline <pattern> <length> <gravity> <noise> [-i <inertia>] [-c <convexSelPoints>] [-s]**`

`**Alias: //flowline**`

Génère une seule ligne de flux en fonction de la position de l'acteur et de la direction de visualisation. Le même principe fondamental qu'un champ de flux, mais en ne générant qu'une seule ligne.

*   **Pattern**: Détermine le motif des blocs à placer.
    
*   **Length**: définit la longueur de la ligne d'écoulement en blocs. Cela définit la distance à laquelle la ligne d'écoulement s'étendra à partir du point de départ.
    
*   **Gravity** (par défaut: -1): applique la gravité aux points, les tirant dans la direction spécifiée.
    
*   **Noise** (par défaut: `Perlin()`): le type de noise utilisé pour générer le champ d'écoulement.flowfield.
    
*   **\-i** (par défaut: 0.0): ajuste la pondération de l'inertie du point, en contrôlant l'influence des directions de mouvement précédentes sur les directions futures. Une valeur comprise entre 0,0 et 1,0.
    
*   **\-c** (par défaut: 0): si la valeur est supérieure à 0, crée une sélection convexe à partir de la ligne de flux, en utilisant le nombre de points spécifié pour définir la forme de la sélection.
    
*   **\-s**: Permet d'accrocher la ligne d'écoulement aux surfaces, faisant adhérer la ligne aux contours du paysage ou des structures qu'elle croise.
    

[PreviousDeformation](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/deformation)
[NextGénération noise](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/noisegen)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [//ezflowfield](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/flowfields#ezflowfield)
    
*   [//ezflowline](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/flowfields#ezflowline)

# Explications Noise | French | ezEdits Wiki

Le bruit peut être un sujet complexe pour quiconque ne l'a jamais étudié auparavant, mais dans ses termes les plus simples, le bruit est un moyen d'obtenir une valeur à partir d'une entrée (généralement des coordonnées X, Y, Z).

L'endroit où vous serez probablement le plus familier avec le bruit est dans la génération de terrain de Minecraft. À chaque point du monde, plusieurs fonctions de bruit sont combinées pour déterminer si un bloc doit être placé, et si oui, quel bloc.

C'est à peu près ce que nous faisons dans ezEdits, en utilisant le bruit pour générer des formes, du terrain et des textures.

Dans le plugin, vous trouverez plusieurs types de bruit, chacun ayant des caractéristiques différentes, et Cellular est spécifiquement livré avec de nombreux paramètres supplémentaires que vous pouvez personnaliser.

Certaines des nombreuses fonctionnalités qui utilisent le bruit incluent :

*   `//eznoisegen ...` - _Commandes Noisegen_
    
*   `#eznoisemask` - _Masques_
    
*   `//ezbrush gradient ...` - _Brushes_
    

_Le bruit dans ezEdits est basé sur une version modifiée de FastNoiseLite, nous recommandons donc fortement ce site Web pour expérimenter les paramètres de bruit :_ [_http://auburn.github.io/FastNoiseLite/_](http://auburn.github.io/FastNoiseLite/)

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/noise/noise-explained#parametres-de-bruit)

Paramètres de bruit


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Chaque paramètre et de nombreuses valeurs disposent également d'un raccourci, tel que « Fractal » au lieu de « FractalType » ou « Simplex » au lieu de « OpenSimplex2 ». Dans la mesure du possible, le raccourci sera indiqué entre parenthèses. `Red = Parameter` `Purple = Value`

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/noise/noise-explained#type-de-bruit)

Type de bruit

Réglage du type de bruit[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/noise/noise-explained#reglage-du-type-de-bruit)

Définit le type de bruit à utiliser. Il s'agit du début de tout bruit et sera au format `Noise()`, par exemple `Perlin()`, où tous les autres paramètres seront placés entre parenthèses.

*   `Perlin (per)`
    
*   `OpenSimplex2 (simplex)`
    
*   `OpenSimplex2S (smooth)`
    
*   `Value (val)`
    
*   `ValueCubic (cubic)`
    
*   `White`
    
*   `Cellular (vor)`
    
*   `Shard`
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/noise/noise-explained#parametres-de-bruit-de-base)

Paramètres de bruit de base

Paramètres de bruit de base[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/noise/noise-explained#parametres-de-bruit-de-base-1)

*   `Seed` Définit la valeur de départ pour le bruit. -1 ou aucune valeur entraînera une valeur de départ de bruit aléatoire.
    
*   `Frequency (Freq)` Définit la fréquence du bruit. Une fréquence plus élevée entraînera un bruit plus prononcé, une valeur plus basse entraînera un bruit plus doux.
    
*   `Inverted (Invert)` Inverser ou non la valeur du bruit. La valeur par défaut est false.
    
    *   `True`
        
    *   `False`
        
    
*   `ValueMapping (Map)` Indique s'il faut ignorer ou remplacer le mappage de valeurs. Par défaut, le bruit est échantillonné pour correspondre à une valeur comprise entre 0 et 1.
    
    *   `Default (Def)`
        
    *   `None (No)`
        
    *   `Override (OR)` **Si annulé :**
        
        *   `LowerBound (Min)`
            
        *   `UpperBound (Max)`
            
        
    
*   `YScaling (Y)` Lors de l'utilisation de bruits 3D, cela peut être utilisé pour étirer ou écraser l'axe Y.
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/noise/noise-explained#parametres-du-bruit-cellulaire)

Paramètres du bruit cellulaire

**Paramètres du bruit cellulaire**[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/noise/noise-explained#parametres-du-bruit-cellulaire-1)

*   `CellularJitterModifier (Jitter)` Contrôle généralement `0..1.0` la gigue aléatoire ou la distribution des nœuds de bruit cellulaire, 0 étant une grille parfaite et 1 étant au maximum « aléatoire », sans chevauchement. Les valeurs supérieures à 1 commenceront à chevaucher leurs voisins.
    
*   `CellularDistanceFunction (Distance)` Contrôle la méthode mathématique utilisée pour déterminer la valeur de distance de chaque point à son nœud.
    
    *   `Euclidean`
        
    *   `EuclideanSq (sq)`
        
    *   `Manhattan (man)`
        
    *   `Hybrid`
        
    *   `Minkovski1 (m1)`
        
    *   `Minkowvki4 (m4)`
        
    *   `Minkowski99 (m99)`
        
    *   `Rounded (round)`
        
    
*   `CellularReturnType (DistReturn)` Contrôle la manière dont la valeur de distance est modifiée avant d'être renvoyée. Toutes les valeurs Distance2\* font référence au deuxième nœud le plus proche au lieu du plus proche.
    
    *   `CellValue (cell)`
        
    *   `Distance (1)`
        
    *   `DistanceSquared (sq)`
        
    *   `DistanceInverse (inv)`
        
    *   `DistanceLog (log)`
        
    *   `DistanceExp (exp)`
        
    *   `Distance2 (2)`
        
    *   `Distance2Add (2add)`
        
    *   `Distance2Add (2sub)`
        
    *   `Distance2Add (2mul)`
        
    *   `Distance2Add (2div)`
        
    *   `Distance2Sq (2sq)`
        
    *   `Distance2Inv (2inv)`
        
    *   `Distance2Log (2log)`
        
    *   `Distance2Exp (2exp)`
        
    *   `Edge`
        
    *   `Rounded (round)`
        
    *   `NoiseLookup (noise)` **Paramètres de recherche de bruit supplémentaires :**
        
        *   `CellularNoiseLookup (Lookup)` Lorsque vous utilisez le type de retour NoiseLookup, cela contrôle le bruit sous-jacent sur lequel superposer le bruit cellulaire.
            
            *   `Perlin (per)`
                
            *   `OpenSimplex2 (simplex)`
                
            *   `OpenSimplex2S (smooth)`
                
            *   `Value (val)`
                
            *   `ValueCubic (cubic)`
                
            *   `White`
                
            *   `Cellular (vor)`
                
            
        *   `CellularNoiseLookupFrequency (DistReturn)` Contrôle la fréquence du bruit sous-jacent.
            
        
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/noise/noise-explained#parametres-du-bruit-des-eclats)

Paramètres du bruit des éclats

Paramètres du bruit des éclats[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/noise/noise-explained#parametres-du-bruit-des-eclats-1)

*   `Sharpness (Sharp)` Contrôle généralement `0..1.0` la netteté du motif pour le bruit des éclats. Les valeurs élevées ont des bords plus définis dans le motif, tandis que les valeurs faibles apparaîtront plus floues.
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/noise/noise-explained#parametres-du-bruit-fractal)

Paramètres du bruit fractal

Paramètres du bruit fractal[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/noise/noise-explained#parametres-du-bruit-fractal-1)

*   `FractalType (Fractal)` Définit le type de bruit fractal à utiliser.
    
    *   `None (No)`
        
    *   `FBm`
        
    *   `Ridged`
        
    *   `PingPong (PP)` **Paramètre fractal PingPong supplémentaire :**
        
        *   `PingPongStrength (PPStr)`
            
        
    

**Si le type fractal est autre que celui sélectionné :**

*   `Octaves (Oct)` Définit le nombre de couches de bruit fractal à utiliser.
    
*   `Lacunarity (Lac)` Définit l'échelle de chaque couche fractale. Les valeurs > 1 augmenteront effectivement la fréquence de chaque couche, les valeurs < 1 réduiront effectivement la fréquence de chaque couche.
    
*   `Gain` Définit la force relative de chaque couche fractale. Les valeurs < 1 diminueront la force de chaque couche, les valeurs > 1 augmenteront.
    
*   `WeightedStrength (Weighted)` Définit la réactivité de la force de chaque couche à la valeur du bruit.
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/noise/noise-explained#parametres-de-deformation-de-domaine)

Paramètres de déformation de domaine

Paramètres de déformation de domaine[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/noise/noise-explained#parametres-de-deformation-de-domaine-1)

*   `DomainWarpType (Warp)` Définit le type de déformation de domaine à utiliser.
    
    *   `None (No)`
        
    *   `BasicGrid (Grid)`
        
    *   `OpenSimplex2 (Simplex)`
        
    *   `OpenSimplex2Reduced (Reduced)`
        
    *   `Flow`
        
    *   `Turbulence (Turb)`
        
    

**Si le type de déformation de domaine est autre que celui sélectionné :**

*   `DomainWarpFreq (WarpFreq)` Définit la fréquence de la déformation du domaine.
    
*   `DomainWarpOct (WarpOct)` Définit le nombre de couches pour la déformation de domaine.
    
*   `DomainWarpGain (WarpGain)` Définit la force relative de chaque couche de déformation de domaine.
    
*   `DomainWarpAmp (WarpAmp)` Définit l'amplitude globale (force) de la déformation du domaine.
    
*   `DomainWarpFrac (WarpFrac)` Définit le type fractal spécifique de déformation de domaine à utiliser.
    
    *   `None (No)`
        
    *   `DomainWarpIndependent (ind)`
        
    *   `DomainWarpProgressive (prog)`
        
    
*   `DomainWarpLacunarity (WarpLac)` Définit l'échelle de chaque couche de déformation de domaine.
    

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/noise/noise-explained#exemples)

# Placement Parameters | ezEdits Wiki

Whenever a structure is placed, it goes through the following pipeline (in that order):

*   [Applying Dimensions](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#dimensions-s)
     (`-s`)
    
*   [Random Scaling](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#random-scaling-o)
     (`-t`)
    
*   [Orientation](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#orientation-c-k)
     (`-c` and `-k`)
    
*   [Random Flips](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#random-flips-f)
     (`-f`)
    
*   [Random 90° Rotations](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#random-rotations-r)
     (`-r`)
    
*   [**Alignment**](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/primary+secondary-alignment)
     (`<primary>` and `<secondary>`)
    

ezEdits lets you fully customize this pipeline. In brackets are the flags and arguments that apply changes to each step respectively.

* * *

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#dimensions-s)

Controlling Dimensions: `-s <dimensions>`

The dimensions define the size of a structure placement, by setting its bounding box size.

The flag `-s <dimensions>` sets the desired absolute base dimensions of the placement (overriding the default values).

By default, expression-based structures have dimensions `20,20,20`, while Schematic/Clipboard structures are placed with their inherent original dimensions.

The structure might appear **stretched** or **compressed** depending on your choice of values.

Example[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#example)

For example, if your clipboard is inherently of size 5x7x5, then setting the dimensions as `-s 5,14,5` will stretch out the structure placement along its y-axis:

First image: `//ezsc Clipboard -s 5,7,5` (original clipboard size)

Second image: `//ezsc Clipboard -s 5,14,5`

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-164f04da551171cc9fa9f0b7b49154fa9a640af7%252FPlacementDimensions_example1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=10cd427&sv=2)![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-b8ffa1bc89404a2414f06181ef57f4738f46f0a4%252FPlacementDimensions_example2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4405e74a&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#random-scaling-o)

Random Scaling: `-o <sizeMultiplierRange>`

Most of the structure commands place multiple structure placements at once. To give a bit of variety you can apply some random scaling for each placement.

The `-o <sizeMultiplierRange>` applies random scaling for each placement. You specify a range of values. A random number from this range is chosen as the scaling factor for each placement.

By default, the range is `1,1`, meaning the scaling factor is always 1, and thus, does nothing.

Example[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#example-1)

By setting the range as `-o 0.5,2.0` we get placements of e.g. our clipboard at random sizes between half the desired size and double the desired size,

`//ezsc Clipboard -o 0.5,2.0`

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-9a7b746019ec9d941bbd4d3fbbfbdc3e7f9ca5cb%252FPlacementRandomScaling_example.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=57f52eac&sv=2)

(Same tree clipboard at various different sizes)

* * *

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#random-flips-f)

Random Flips: `-f <randomFlipsAxes>`

The `-f <randomFlipsAxes>` flag enables random flipping of the structure across any of the axes for each placement.

Available values are:

*   None (default)
    
*   X
    
*   Y
    
*   Z
    
*   XY
    
*   XZ
    
*   YZ
    
*   XYZ
    

Flips are applied after orientation but before alignment.

Example[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#example-2)

First Image: `//ezsc Clipboard` (no random flips)

Second Image: `//ezsc Clipboard -f XZ` (random mirrors along x- and z-axis, but not y)

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-a7d6d873db9fdc4f2813c25b0fa7d1828f4d20ac%252FPlacementRandomFlips_example1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=33b10878&sv=2)![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-b7615a3f0298f318d912ef1beb7078a49a9a6e45%252FPlacementRandomFlips_example2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a0ad1a8&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#random-rotations-r)

Random 90°-Rotations: `-r <randomRotationAxis>`

The `-r <randomRotationAxis>` flag enables random 90° rotation of the structure across either of the axes for each placement.

Available values are:

*   X
    
*   Y
    
*   Z
    

By default, this parameter is not set to anything, i.e. random rotations are disabled.

90°-rotations are applied after orientation but before alignment.

Example[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#example-3)

First Image: `//ezsc Clipboard` (no random rotations)

Second Image: `//ezsc Clipboard -r Y` (random 90°-rotations around the y-axis)

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-0da24532bc0b9c0baed70302ec66adbad6ff84a0%252FPlacementRandomRotations_example1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=44e3ebf1&sv=2)![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-354be798314a340eb84d24b46e768c908019917d%252FPlacementRandomRotations_example2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f8ef911c&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#orientation-c-k)

Orientation (advanced): `-k <orientationAxis>` and `-c <orientationAngle>`

Setting an orientation means defining which internal coordinate system the structure has. That coordinate system is then used in the random flips/rotations and during alignment. _Defining an orientation is "defining which way is up and which way is forward"_

Orientation is set by a rotation axis (`-k <direction>`) and a rotation angle (`-c <angle>`). _The rotation works identically to_ `_//ezd rotate_`

By default, the rotation axis `-k` is `y` or `up` and the rotation angle `-c` is `0`, which means no rotation.

For example, if you set the rotation axis to `-k x` and the rotation angle to `-c 90` then your structure is rotated to the side. Its eastern side will now be the "up-direction" and so on.

* * *

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#place-air-a)

Place Air: `-a`

By default, if this flag _is not_ set, air blocks are skipped when placing a structure. When this flag _is_ set, air blocks within the structure are able to override existing blocks.

This behaviour is opposite to `//paste`'s `-a` flag. It may be confusing, but we think it's more convenient for our commands.

[PreviousPrimary+Secondary Alignment](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/primary+secondary-alignment)
[NextScatter Parameters](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/scatter-parameters)

Last updated 10 months ago

*   [Random Flips: -f <randomFlipsAxes>](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#random-flips-f)
    
*   [Random 90°-Rotations: -r <randomRotationAxis>](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#random-rotations-r)

# 调色板命令 | Chinese | ezEdits Wiki

所有子命令都在 `//ezpalette` (`//ezp`) 命令下 例如 `//ezpalette list`

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/zh_cn/tiao-se-ban/palette-commands#ezpalette)

`//ezpalette ...`


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/zh_cn/tiao-se-ban/palette-commands#fetch-less-than-fetchmode-greater-than-less-than-palettename-greater-than-length-d-less-than-directi)

`fetch <fetchMode> <paletteName> [length] [-d <direction>] [-f]`

获取调色板[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/zh_cn/tiao-se-ban/palette-commands#huo-qu-tiao-se-ban)

保存一个用户定义的调色板并为其指定一个名称。

*   **获取模式**: 从哪里获取调色板中的方块：
    
    *   `**WORLD**`
        
        *   从玩家的位置获取方块。
            
        
    *   `**SELECTION**`
        
        *   从玩家的选择区域获取方块。
            
        *   选择区域必须为 1x1xN 大小，其中 N 是所需的调色板长度。
            
        
    *   `**HOTBAR**`
        
        *   从玩家的快捷栏中获取方块。
            
        *   忽略物品并使用默认的方块属性。
            
        
    
*   **长度** (默认值: 0): 要获取的方块数量。长度为 0（默认值）将获取方块，直到遇到空气为止。
    
*   **\-d** (默认值: me): 获取的方向。默认值为用户面对的方向。
    
*   **\-f**: 激活时，覆盖同名现有调色板。
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2203755917-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FprArdPVTMFbs2Ewnf2OB%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-0a1136769ebd73313aeb3f1513411521a7c725d7%252Fezp_fetch.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cbdce0a6&sv=2)

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/zh_cn/tiao-se-ban/palette-commands#save-less-than-palettename-greater-than-less-than-palette-greater-than-f)

`save <paletteName> <palette> [-f]`

保存具有指定名称的用户定义调色板。

*   **\-f**: 激活时，覆盖具有相同名称的现有调色板。
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/zh_cn/tiao-se-ban/palette-commands#delete-less-than-palettename-greater-than)

`delete <paletteName>`

删除与指定名称匹配的用户定义调色板。

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/zh_cn/tiao-se-ban/palette-commands#list-set)

`list [SET]`

*   `ALL` 列出所有可用的调色板
    
*   `DEFAULT` 列出所有默认的插件调色板
    
*   `MINE` 列出所有用户定义的调色板
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/zh_cn/tiao-se-ban/palette-commands#place-less-than-palette-greater-than-direction)

`place <palette> [direction]`

在指定方向上将调色板作为一行方块放置在世界中。 方向默认是用户面朝的方向。

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/zh_cn/tiao-se-ban/palette-commands#swap-less-than-sourcepalette-greater-than-less-than-targetpalette-greater-than-a-f)

`swap <sourcePalette> <targetPalette> [-a] [-f]`

区域操作，将源调色板的方块与目标调色板的方块交换。

*   **\-a**: 激活以包括空气方块（如果源调色板包含空气）。
    
*   **\-f**: 激活以拉伸目标调色板以匹配源调色板的大小。
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/zh_cn/tiao-se-ban/palette-commands#print-less-than-palette-greater-than-v)

`print <palette> [-v]`

在聊天中打印给定调色板的方块。方块列表可以点击复制。

**\-v**: 详细模式。将打印完整的方块名称和方块状态。

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/zh_cn/tiao-se-ban/palette-commands#encode-less-than-palette-greater-than)

`encode <palette>`

打印表示给定调色板的编码字符串。点击字符串即可复制。 _仅支持原版Minecraft方块。_

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/zh_cn/tiao-se-ban/palette-commands#decode-less-than-string-greater-than)

`decode <string>`

打印给定编码调色板字符串的方块。方块列表可以点击复制。

[Previous调色板说明](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/zh_cn/tiao-se-ban/palettes-explained)
[Next噪声说明](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/zh_cn/zao-sheng/zao-sheng-shuo-ming)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Surface | French | ezEdits Wiki

Toutes les sous-commandes sont sous `//ezsurface` (`//ezsu`) par exemple`//ezsurface rockify`

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/surface#ezsurface)

`//ezsurface ...`


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/surface#fuzzify)

`fuzzify`

Fuzzify Surface[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/surface#fuzzify-surface)

`**//ezsu fuzzify <radius> [smooth_radius] [smooth_iterations] [-c] [-e] [-m] [-t]**`

Utilise du noise blanc pour rendre la surface plus floue.

*   **Radius**: Valeur flottante déterminant la distance maximale de la surface à laquelle des modifications peuvent se produire.
    
*   **Smooth Radius** (par défaut: 0): spécifie le rayon pour les opérations de lissage.
    
*   **Smooth Iterations** (par défaut: 0): détermine le nombre de fois que l'opération de lissage est appliquée.
    
*   **\-c**: limite les modifications à la sculpture sur le terrain uniquement.
    
*   **\-e**: limite l'opération à l'extension uniquement à partir du terrain.
    
*   **\-m**: applique un masque pour modifier uniquement les surfaces qui correspondent aux critères spécifiés. Cette option peut ralentir considérablement le processus en raison de la complexité supplémentaire de la correspondance des surfaces.
    
*   **\-t**: Tente de conserver la topologie de la région..
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/surface#rockify)

`rockify`

Rockify Surface[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/surface#rockify-surface)

`**//ezsu rockify <radius> [size] [oct] [smooth_radius] [smooth_iterations] [-c] [-e] [-m] [-t]**`

Utilise le noise Perlin pour rendre une surface rocheuse.

*   **Radius**: Valeur flottante déterminant la distance maximale de la surface à laquelle des modifications peuvent se produire.
    
*   **Noise Size** (par défaut: 10): contrôle l’échelle du noise utilisé.
    
*   **Noise Octaves** (par défaut: 1): définit le nombre de couches de noise appliquées.
    
*   **Smooth Radius** (par défaut: 1): spécifie le rayon pour les opérations de lissage.
    
*   **Smooth Iterations** (par défaut: 4): détermine le nombre de fois que l'opération de lissage est appliquée.
    
*   **\-c**: limite les modifications à la sculpture sur le terrain uniquement.
    
*   **\-e**: limite l'opération à l'extension uniquement à partir du terrain.
    
*   **\-m**: applique un masque pour modifier uniquement les surfaces qui correspondent aux critères spécifiés. Cette option peut ralentir considérablement le processus en raison de la complexité supplémentaire de la correspondance des surfaces.
    
*   **\-t**: Tente de conserver la topologie de la région.
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/surface#voronoify)

`voronoify`

Voronoify Surface[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/surface#voronoify-surface)

`**//ezsu voronoify <radius> [cell_size] [smooth_radius] [smooth_iterations] [-c] [-e] [-m] [-t]**`

Utilise le noise de Voronoi pour déformer une surface.

*   **Radius**: Valeur flottante déterminant la distance maximale de la surface à laquelle des modifications peuvent se produire.
    
*   **Cell Size** (par défaut: 12): spécifie le rayon pour les opérations de lissage.
    
*   **Smooth Radius** (par défaut: 0): Specifies the radius for smoothing operations.
    
*   **Smooth Iterations** (par défaut: 0): détermine le nombre de fois que l'opération de lissage est appliquée.
    
*   **\-c**: limite les modifications à la sculpture sur le terrain uniquement.
    
*   **\-e**: limite l'opération à l'extension uniquement à partir du terrain.
    
*   **\-m**: applique un masque pour modifier uniquement les surfaces qui correspondent aux critères spécifiés. Cette option peut ralentir considérablement le processus en raison de la complexité supplémentaire de la correspondance des surfaces.
    
*   **\-t**: Tente de conserver la topologie de la région.
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/surface#noisify)

`noisify`

Noiseify Surface[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/surface#noiseify-surface)

`**//ezsu noisify <radius> <noise> [scale] [smooth_radius] [smooth_iterations] [-c] [-e] [-m] [-t]**`

Utilise un préréglage de noise pour déformer une surface.

*   **Radius**: Valeur flottante déterminant la distance maximale de la surface à laquelle des modifications peuvent se produire.
    
*   **Noise**: Spécifie le noise à utiliser pour la modification.
    
*   **Scale** (par défaut: 1): ajuste l’échelle du noise.
    
*   **Smooth Radius** (par défaut: 1): spécifie le rayon pour les opérations de lissage.
    
*   **Smooth Iterations** (par défaut: 4): détermine le nombre de fois que l'opération de lissage est appliquée.
    
*   **\-c**: limite les modifications à la sculpture sur le terrain uniquement.
    
*   **\-e**: limite l'opération à l'extension uniquement à partir du terrain.
    
*   **\-m**:applique un masque pour modifier uniquement les surfaces qui correspondent aux critères spécifiés. Cette option peut ralentir considérablement le processus en raison de la complexité supplémentaire de la correspondance des surfaces.
    
*   **\-t**: Tente de conserver la topologie de la région.
    

[PreviousVitre colorée](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/stained-glass)
[NextTexture](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/french/commandes/texturing)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Deformation | ezEdits Wiki

Deformation commands deform the contents of the given region into new shapes and forms.

All sub-commands are under `//ezdeform` (`//ezd`) e.g `//ezdeform hexagonalize`

* * *

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/deformation#list-of-subcommands)

List of subcommands


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

#### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/deformation#undefined)

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-f94534ef45825812589208b925839c97595ccb3c%252Fezdeform_hexagonalize_xrot.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=333e8ab7&sv=2)

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/deformation#ezdeform-hexagonalize)

` //ezdeform`` ` `hexagonalize`

Hexagonalize[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/deformation#hexagonalize)

`**//ezdeform hexagonalize [**``**size**``**] [**``**air_gap**``**] [**``**x_rotation**``**] [**``**z_rotation**``**] [**``**offset_angle**``**] [**``**-w <profile>**``**]**`

Deforms the region into hexagonal columns.

*   **Size** (Default: 12): Sets the size of hexagons.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-3c09a245c9b8d1b4b1e874565d7bd72bb9bd351b%252Fezdeform_hexagonalize_size.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=405ada9f&sv=2)

*   **Air Gap** (Default: 0.0): Defines the width of the air gap between columns.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-734668222a990e4d52c78b53214c61f7ce6e5a62%252Fezdeform_hexagonalize_airgap.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=50dafffb&sv=2)

*   **X Rotation** (Default: 0.0): Sets the column rotation angle along the X-axis, in degrees.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-f94534ef45825812589208b925839c97595ccb3c%252Fezdeform_hexagonalize_xrot.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=333e8ab7&sv=2)

*   **Z Rotation** (Default: 0.0): Sets the column rotation angle along the Z-axis, in degrees.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-826af981fb0bedcab48d1cdd8e0b6b835dd4cba5%252Fezdeform_hexagonalize_zrot.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ad9f5862&sv=2)

*   **Offset Angle** (Default: 60.0): Adjusts the offset angle, controlling the shape (range: 0-90 degrees).
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-c3d67f2ab63ae9c7d3e3a21a5da68103031a40f2%252Fezdeform_hexagonalize_shape.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5d478b7b&sv=2)

*   **\-w**: See [Smoothblocks](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/smoothblocks/smoothblocks)
    .
    

* * *

#### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/deformation#undefined-1)

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-45d6110e1f34110f21c6d4353803a801e3d5b6ae%252Fezdeform_noise.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cd473724&sv=2)

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/deformation#ezdeform-noise)

` //ezdeform`` ` `noise`

Noise[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/deformation#noise)

`**//ezdeform noise <**``**noise**``**> [**``**strength**``**] [**``**-z <zoom>**``**] [**``**-s <seed>**``**] [**``**-w <profile>**``**]**`

Deforms region according the given noise field.

*   **Noise**: Specifies the type of noise to use for deformation.
    

*   **Strength** (Default: 2.0): Sets the strength of the noise effect.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-c632673a2b2efb0a303e702bb3835e133293b5d8%252Fezdeform_noise_strength.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7775b2d0&sv=2)

*   **Zoom** (Default: 1): Determines the scale of the noise.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-f0774e98da3a6ff6e29b7218054c60c9a6e3feb6%252Fezdeform_noise_frequency.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=67f0b687&sv=2)

*   **\-s <seed>** (Default: -1): Optional seed for the noise pattern.
    
*   **\-h**: When used, only deforms the region horizontally.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-27a98227f34e2c133db73dfe29afb57e60192e1e%252Fezdeform_noise_hflag.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=87e24dc5&sv=2)

*   **\-v**: When used, only deforms the region vertically.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-a0be3e99c7ce10b61a23b0637b25ca9c9c5a0630%252Fezdeform_noise_vflag.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bfce127e&sv=2)

*   **\-w**: See [Smoothblocks](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/smoothblocks/smoothblocks)
    .
    

* * *

#### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/deformation#undefined-2)

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-d539301e6aa6e451f6b71e4bccffcdf85d9d88f6%252Fezdeform_rotate_angle.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bcc552e7&sv=2)

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/deformation#ezdeform-rotate)

` //ezdeform`` ` `rotate`

Rotate[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/deformation#rotate)

`**//ezdeform rotate <**``**angle**``**> [**``**-o**``**] [**``**-w <profile>**``**]**`

Rotates region clockwise with the the center of rotation being the center of the selection (or the player's head position using -o) and with the player aim defining the axis of rotation.

*   **Angle**: Sets the angle of rotation, in degrees.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-d539301e6aa6e451f6b71e4bccffcdf85d9d88f6%252Fezdeform_rotate_angle.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bcc552e7&sv=2)

*   **\-o**: When used, uses the player's position as the center of rotation instead of the selection's center.
    
*   **\-w**: See [Smoothblocks](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/smoothblocks/smoothblocks)
    .
    

* * *

#### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/deformation#undefined-3)

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-755b5702850f2aba20ee40185b5ad12118c595ba%252Fezdeform_voronoialize_airgap.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e5af891&sv=2)

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/deformation#ezdeform-voronoialize)

` //ezdeform`` ` `voronoialize`

Voronoialize[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/deformation#voronoialize)

`**//ezdeform voronoialize [**``**size**``**] [**``**air_gap**``**] [**``**-s <seed>**``**] [**``**-w <profile>**``**]**`

Deforms region to randomly distributed voronoi cells.

*   **Size** (Default: 12): Determines the size of the voronoi cells.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-0a84845b23c611dd0ffd56c5bb59abd87b9179bf%252Fezdeform_voronoialize_size.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2a169a0b&sv=2)

*   **Air Gap** (Default: 0.0): Specifies the width of the air gap between cells.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-755b5702850f2aba20ee40185b5ad12118c595ba%252Fezdeform_voronoialize_airgap.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e5af891&sv=2)

*   **\-s <seed>** (Default: -1): Optional seed for generating the pattern.
    
*   **\-w <profile>**: See [Smoothblocks](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/smoothblocks/smoothblocks)
    .
    

* * *

#### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/deformation#undefined-4)

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-3647d7618006dc738932ddae1e8491f04692c51e%252Fezdeform_voronoialize2_airgap.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a5945c1f&sv=2)

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/deformation#ezdeform-voronoialize2)

` //ezdeform`` ` `voronoialize2`

Alternative Voronoialize[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/deformation#alternative-voronoialize)

`**//ezdeform voronoialize2 <**``**amount**``**> [**``**air_gap**``**] [**``**-s <seed>**``**] [**``**-r <uniformity>**``**] [**``**-n <normalOffset>**``**] [**``**-w <profile>**``**]**`

Deforms the region to Voronoi cells distributed along the surface shape. Could more accurately preserve the original shape compared to the first voronoialize.

*   **Amount**: Specifies the cell amount in the voronoi pattern. A small amount naturally leads to larger cells and vice versa.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-75f3897b30f6620a2f6fca6d7947ba5c6e038d93%252Fezdeform_voronoialize2_amount.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4b47a974&sv=2)

*   **Air Gap** (Default: 0.0): Determines the width of the air gap between cells.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-3647d7618006dc738932ddae1e8491f04692c51e%252Fezdeform_voronoialize2_airgap.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a5945c1f&sv=2)

*   **\-s <seed>** (Default: -1): Optional seed for generating the pattern. `-1` will randomly generate a seed.
    
*   **\-r <uniformity>** (Default: 15): Sets the voronoi seed point repulsion iteration count. 0 means fully random. 15 iterations lead to a more uniform/even appearance.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-3b6a47ba05ef61676b13eaea1cfb44210af79bc0%252Fezdeform_voronoialize2_repulsion.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d60d51ef&sv=2)

*   **\-n <normalOffset>** (Default: 5): Technical parameter. Adjusts how deep the cell seed is positioned into the shape. Larger/Thicker shapes could benefit from a larger value. Thinner shapes should use a smaller value if the generation breaks down.
    
*   **\-w <profile>**: See [Smoothblocks](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/smoothblocks/smoothblocks)
    .
    

* * *

#### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/deformation#undefined-5)

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-112f4cda4e6ed00d8d6c1409f07af53bfe577e63%252Fezdeform_voxelize_scales.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e642a824&sv=2)

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/deformation#ezdeform-voxelize)

` //ezdeform`` ` `voxelize`

Voxelize[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/deformation#voxelize)

`**//ezdeform voxelize <**``**scales**``**> <**``**gap**``**> <**``**distortion**``**> [**``**-i <primary>**``**] [**``**-j <secondary>**``**] [**``**-s <seed>**``**] [**``**-hv**``**] [**``**-w <profile>**``**]**`

Deforms region into larger cuboid shapes.

*   **Scales** (Default: 3): Sets the scale of the cuboids.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-112f4cda4e6ed00d8d6c1409f07af53bfe577e63%252Fezdeform_voxelize_scales.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e642a824&sv=2)

You may put three comma-separated values to define the dimension for each axis. ![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-5898d2be357d2147b75a7e8f528cd2d2576590dd%252Fezdeform_voxelize_scales3.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f6dfd2f&sv=2)

*   **Gap** (Default: 0.0): Defines the width of the air gap between voxels.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-caf15180a420aa2a3b168f90eeb47290bb023d1e%252Fezdeform_voxelize_airgap.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d3a5df39&sv=2)

*   **Distortion** (Default: 0.0): Adjusts the strength of random grid distortion (range: 0-1).
    

*   **\-s <seed>** (Default: -1): Optional seed for the distortion.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-e6b9588be99bf9819eb0429c732673f13ae78c4c%252Fezdeform_voxelize_distortion.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e56ba92a&sv=2)

*   **\-i <primary>** (Default: y): Specifies the y-axis direction for grid.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-6d5b4eba477f90b4780fffbe34c9f1b6dc980041%252Fezdeform_voxelize_primary.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b3b83d5d&sv=2)

*   **\-j <secondary>** (Default: -x): Specifies the x-axis direction of the grid.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-516f03bec29a26ad9ddd903b40f2991314495f1d%252Fezdeform_voxelize_secondary.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=57769e53&sv=2)

*   **\-h**: When used, only voxelizes horizontally.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-8a0efabffdcb446c3db5a0a2d76bb8ec01c19373%252Fezdeform_voxelize_hflag1.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8bdd646e&sv=2)

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-bbb82e79e5fe02712b2859d4335afb50c330a883%252Fezdeform_voxelize_hflag2.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4813a924&sv=2)

*   **\-v**: When used, only voxelizes vertically.
    

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-35265b442696ee77fe61691f37f4a7a75c78af3c%252Fezdeform_voxelize_vflag1.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7550ddd&sv=2)

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-519e4c9565d733196489f51efc85f204de55454f%252Fezdeform_voxelize_vflag2.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=807674bb&sv=2)

*   **\-w**: See [Smoothblocks](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/smoothblocks/smoothblocks)
    .

# 噪声命令 | Chinese | ezEdits Wiki

所有指令都在主命令 `//eznoise` (`//ezn`) 下 例如 `//eznoise list`

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/zh_cn/zao-sheng/noise-commands#eznoise)

`//eznoise ...`


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/zh_cn/zao-sheng/noise-commands#list-set)

`list [SET]`

*   `ALL` 列出所有可用的噪声预设
    
*   `DEFAULT` 列出所有默认的插件噪声预设
    
*   `MINE` 列出所有用户定义的噪声预设
    

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/zh_cn/zao-sheng/noise-commands#save-less-than-presetname-greater-than-less-than-noise-greater-than-f)

`save <presetName> <noise> [-f]`

使用给定的名称保存用户定义的噪声预设。 使用 `-f` 可以覆盖现有的噪声预设。

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/zh_cn/zao-sheng/noise-commands#delete-less-than-presetname-greater-than)

`delete <presetName>`

删除与给定名称匹配的用户定义噪声预设。

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/zh_cn/zao-sheng/noise-commands#print-less-than-noise-greater-than)

`print <noise>`

在聊天中打印给定噪声预设的设置。

[Previous噪声说明](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/zh_cn/zao-sheng/zao-sheng-shuo-ming)
[Next蒙板](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/zh_cn/meng-ban-he-tu-an/masks)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [//eznoise ...](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/zh_cn/zao-sheng/noise-commands#eznoise)
    
*   [list \[SET\]](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/zh_cn/zao-sheng/noise-commands#list-set)
    
*   [save <presetName> <noise> \[-f\]](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/zh_cn/zao-sheng/noise-commands#save-less-than-presetname-greater-than-less-than-noise-greater-than-f)
    
*   [delete <presetName>](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/zh_cn/zao-sheng/noise-commands#delete-less-than-presetname-greater-than)

# Array Parameters | ezEdits Wiki

[`//ezarray`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement#overview)
 and [`//ezbrush array`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement#overview)
 place multiple shapes along a path. The following parameters apply to these commands:

* * *

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/array-parameters#distance-g)

Distance: `-g <gap>`

Control how close all placements are by defining the gap distance between each placement.

Defaults to `0`. Meaning, in a straight line each placement comes right after another with no gap.

Positive values will increase that distance and place fewer structures in total. Negative values cause the placements to overlap.

Examples[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/array-parameters#examples)

` //ezarray Clipboard`` `` ``**-g <gap>**` (with the clipboard being a default vanilla oak tree for no particular reason)

` //ezar Cl`` `` ``**-g 0**` : (default value, placements are right next to each other)

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-641d937eedd78b42c05f5633f966f90a45a9c7e2%252FArrayGap_example1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=58ae710d&sv=2)

` //ezar Cl`` `` ``**-g 10**` : (placements are now further apart)

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-deaafd96284afdb2d97440549b8740d58d3635e8%252FArrayGap_example2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d3e73e6e&sv=2)

` //ezar Cl`` `` ``**-g -3**` (negative values cause placements to overlap)

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-8cf9446ee7482ed0154a1c41d70b8d3e56946a87%252FArrayGap_example3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=76d64e15&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/array-parameters#max-vertical-offset-y)

Max Vertical Offset: `-y <maxOffset>`

Enables you to limit the vertical distance between neighbouring placement positions by shifting the placement position vertically.

Specifically made to generate Jump'n'Runs. For example, by doing `-y 1`, each placement position is never higher than 1 block than the previous position. This is only an upper limit in one direction though.

(Introduced in 0.14.0)

Examples[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/array-parameters#examples-1)

`//ezar Cl -g 1` vs `//ezar Cl -g 1` `**-y 1**`

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-06c2aa37ae161ce2cf92f6f900250e490d0e3b66%252FArray_maxYOffset_example1.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=91d0c61d&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/array-parameters#progressive-scaling-q)

Progressive Scaling: `-q <radii>`

Similar to [Random Scaling](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#random-scaling-o)
, this modifier allows scaling of the placements using relative values, e.g. 1 keeps the scale as is, 2 doubles the size, and 0.5 halfs the size.

The scaling factors are defined as a progression along the spline. This means you may specify as many comma-separated scaling factors as you like, and the spline path will smoothly interpolate through all entries.

The syntax is the same as in //ezspline: [Radius progression: <radii>](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/spline/common-parameters#radii)

Examples[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/array-parameters#examples-2)

` //ezarray Clipboard`` `` ``**-q <radii>**`

` //ezar Cl`` `` ``**-q 1**`

(default value, no scaling applied)

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-641d937eedd78b42c05f5633f966f90a45a9c7e2%252FArrayGap_example1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=58ae710d&sv=2)

` //ezar Cl`` `` ``**-q 0.3,3**`

(placements are down-scaled by a factor of 0.3 at the beginning of the path and slowly get bigger up to triple their original size towards the end of the spline path)

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-4282cac18b0b0214f1568db2d66fdff119ac87ea%252FArrayScaling_example2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1752b1e7&sv=2)

` //ezar Cl`` `` ``**-q 1.5,0.5,5.0,2.0,0.2**`

(Tree is being scaled progressively through all given values throughout the spline path)

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-745e8a767b9fda8571631bc70f72d55f544050dd%252FArrayScaling_example3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a047e7b1&sv=2)

` //ezar Cl`` `` ``**-q 1.5,0.5,5.0,2.0,0.2 -o 0.7,1.3**`

(Combining progressive scaling -q with [random scaling](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#random-scaling-o)
 -o)

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-5e98c76b1b51f23c82ab9b16ac00223928f230c5%252FArrayScaling_example4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=35a5ef3a&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/array-parameters#path-parameters-p)

Path Parameters: `-p <kbParameters>`

Modifies how the path is created from the input (convex selection) points.

See //ezspline documentation: [Kochanek-Bartels-Parameters: -p <kbParameters>](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/spline/common-parameters#kb-parameters)

* * *

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/array-parameters#spline-orientation-n)

Spline orientation: `-n <normalMode>`

Modifies how the ORTHOGONAL option for the `<primary>` and `<secondary>` arguments behave.

See //ezspline documentation: [Normal Mode: -n <normalMode>](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/spline/common-parameters#normal-mode)

Examples[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/array-parameters#examples-3)

`//ezarray Clipboard Orthogonal Constant``**-n <normalMode>**`

` //ezar Cl O C`` `` ``**-n CONSISTENT**`

(default value)

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-6b60af89162824db39caaaf6af4f77716ebb3373%252FOrthogonalAlignment_example1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e9dbf048&sv=2)

` //ezar Cl O C`` `` ``**-n UPRIGHT**`

(placements are not as tilted anymore)

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-09ddde9fe383b38041a6fe9a6a981901b5f2d1d7%252FOrthogonalAlignment_example2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=838842d0&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/array-parameters#snap-to-surfaces-b)

Snap placements to surfaces: `-b`

By default, structures are placed along the spline path that's induced by the input (convex selection) points. This flag moves the placement positions to the nearest surface block instead, in case the position on the path is in midair or submerged in blocks.

By default the maximum search range is 96 blocks. The maximum search range can be set in the config. If no surface block is found within that range, the original position will be used instead.

Example[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/array-parameters#example)

GIF comparing

`//ezarray Clipboard` (placements are placed along path)

` //ezarray Clipboard`` `` ``**-b**` (placements positions moved to nearest surface block)

![](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F62542430-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmwyNbIIrWCkyIco2qJ9j%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-b698975b9402dec5a9821f1600fb2c0e8c56be34%252Fezgif.com-animated-gif-maker.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ad997dfe&sv=2)

* * *

[PreviousScatter Parameters](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/scatter-parameters)
[NextSelections](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/selections)

# Placement | ezEdits Wiki

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement#overview)

Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

ezEdits provides multiple ways to quickly and precisely place clipboards, schematics, and expression-based shapes, which we refer to as 'structures'.

The relevant commands and brushes (introduced in version 0.12.0) are:

Command / Brush

`**//ezplace**`

Abbreviation

`**//ezpl**`

Description

Places a **single** structure at the **player's position.**

Syntax

`//ezplace` [`<structure>`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/available-structures)
 [`[<primary>][<secondary>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/primary+secondary-alignment)

Parameters

Accepts [Placement Parameters](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters)
.

Command / Brush

`**//ezbrush place**`

Abbreviation

`**//ezbr pl**`

Description

Brush that places a **single** structure at each **brush click's target**.

Syntax

`//ezbrush place` [`<structure>`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/available-structures)
 [`[<primary>] [<secondary>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/primary+secondary-alignment)

Parameters

Accepts [Placement Parameters](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters)
.

Command / Brush

`**//ezscatter**`

Abbreviation

`**//ezsc**`

Description

Places **multiple** structures within a **selected region**.

Syntax

`//ezscatter`[`<structure>`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/available-structures)
 [`[<primary>] [<secondary>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/primary+secondary-alignment)

Parameters

Accepts [Placement Parameters](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters)
 and [Scatter Parameters](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/scatter-parameters)
.

Command / Brush

`**//ezbrush scatter**`

Abbreviation

`**//ezbr sc**`

Description

Brush that places **multiple** structures in the area of each **brush click's target**.

Syntax

`//ezbrush scatter`[`<structure>`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/available-structures)
 [`[<primary>] [<secondary>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/primary+secondary-alignment)

Parameters

Accepts [Placement Parameters](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters)
 and [Scatter Parameters](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/scatter-parameters)
.

Command / Brush

`**//ezarray**`

Abbreviation

`**//ezar**`

Description

Places **multiple** structures sequentially **along a path**.

Syntax

`//ezarray`[`<structure>`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/available-structures)
 [`[<primary>][<secondary>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/primary+secondary-alignment)

Parameters

Accepts [Placement Parameters](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters)
 and [Array Parameters](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/array-parameters)
.

Command / Brush

`**//ezbrush array**`

Abbreviation

`**//ezbr ar**`

Description

Brush that places **multiple** structures along a **brush stroke**.

Syntax

`//ezbrush array`[`<structure>`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/available-structures)
 [`[<primary>] [<secondary>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/primary+secondary-alignment)

Parameters

Accepts [Placement Parameters](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters)
 and [Array Parameters](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/array-parameters)
.

All six commands are based on the same underlying placement method. As a result, all six commands share the same syntax and parameters.

For completeness, one can also embed a structure or an array of structures into a shaped spline with the ezspline subcommand `//ezspline structure` (`//ezsp structure`). However, the structures are not "placed" as much as they are embedded into the spline path, meaning that the [alignment settings](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/primary+secondary-alignment)
 and the [placement parameters](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters)
 do not apply to that command. Which is why it is documented on the [splines page](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/spline)
 instead.

* * *

[](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement#subpage-structure)

Subpage structure


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This Placement wiki has multiple subpages. Below you find an overview of the subpages.

We suggest reading the [**Primary+Secondary Alignment**](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/primary+secondary-alignment)
 page more carefully, as it covers one of the fundamental concepts of the tools. The remaining chapters can be treated as reference materials, useful for specific tasks or to delve deeper into the tool's capabilities.

*   [**Available Structures**](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/available-structures)
    
    *   Covers the [`<structure>`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/available-structures)
         parameter (necessary for place/scatter/array (and ezspline structure)).
        
    
*   [**Primary+Secondary Alignment**](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/primary+secondary-alignment)
    
    *   Covers the [`[<primary>] [<secondary>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/primary+secondary-alignment)
         parameters (available for place/scatter/array) and the accompanying flags:
        
        *   [`[-j <snapDirections>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/primary+secondary-alignment#snap-to-angles-j)
            
        *   [`[-x]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/primary+secondary-alignment#perturb-secondary-x)
            
        
    
*   [**Placement Parameters**](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters)
    
    *   Covers the following flags (available for place/scatter/array):
        
        *   [`[-s <dimensions>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#dimensions-s)
            
        *   [`[-o <sizeMultiplierRange>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#random-scaling-o)
            
        *   [`[-c <orientationAngle>] [-k <orientationAxis>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#orientation-c-k)
            
        *   [`[-f <randomFlipsAxes>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#random-flips-f)
            
        *   [`[-r <randomRotationAxis>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#random-rotations-r)
            
        *   [`[-a]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/placement-parameters#place-air-a)
            
        
    
*   [**Scatter Parameters**](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/scatter-parameters)
    
    *   Covers the following flags (only available for scatter):
        
        *   [`[-h <region>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/scatter-parameters#scatter-region-h)
            
        *   [`[-d <filterDirections>] [-e <filterThreshold>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/scatter-parameters#directional-filter-d-e)
            
        *   [`[-m <maskFilter>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/scatter-parameters#mask-filter-m)
            
        *   [`[-n <density>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/scatter-parameters#density-n)
            
        *   [`[-i <seed>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/scatter-parameters#distribution-seed-i)
            
        *   [`[-u <iterations>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/scatter-parameters#uniformity-u)
            
        *   [`[-l <coverPattern>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/scatter-parameters#mask-cover-pattern-l)
            
        *   [`[-t]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/scatter-parameters#trim-outside-selection-t)
            
        
    
*   [**Array Parameters**](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/array-parameters)
    
    *   Covers the following flags (only available for array):
        
        *   [`[-g <gap>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/array-parameters#distance-g)
            
        *   [`[-y <maxOffset>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/array-parameters#max-vertical-offset-y)
            
        *   [`[-q <radiiMultiplier>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/array-parameters#progressive-scaling-q)
            
        *   [`[-p <kbParameters>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/array-parameters#path-parameters-p)
            
        *   [`[-n <normalMode>]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/array-parameters#spline-orientation-n)
            
        *   [`[-b]`](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/array-parameters#snap-to-surfaces-b)

* * *

Note for server admins: The three placement brushes spawn BlockDisplay entities (only visible to the player using their brush) to help visualise the [Alignment](https://ezedits.gitbook.io/ezedits/commands/placement/primary+secondary-alignment)
 of the brushes. You may disable the visualisation entities entirely or change how often they are updated in the `config.yml` under `visualisations`.

Additionally, the command `//ezdebug removeVisualiserEntities` will remove any entities spawned by ezEdits from your world in case they got bugged somehow and were not despawned correctly, which should never happen, but there you go.

* * *
